         ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿  i n t r o ! ฿฿฿ฐ฿ฐ     ฿      ฿
                                          ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Road Rebel                                                    บ
 บ    Subject : Introduction to RCN #21                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am writing this to say a few words about RCN and how people treat   บ
 บ  us.  First of all, when you see an article that rips on someone or a      บ
 บ  group, and you don't like it.  Take it up with the author!!!  If it       บ
 บ  isn't written by Rebel Chicken, Hitex or I then don't nag us about it!    บ
 บ  Also, if you have a problem with something written about you or a group,  บ
 บ  WRITE A REBUTTLE!  Don't sit there and bitch at us in the channel, it     บ
 บ  doesn't do shit.  I came to #RCN today, and all I heard was bitching      บ
 บ  because someone said something mean about a group.  WELL, if you are a    บ
 บ  group member and your group gets made fun of, take it on the chin, be a   บ
 บ  man.  We have and will make fun of A LOT of people, most of it is just    บ
 บ  FUN and in MAD RCN, and people realize this and get over it.  If you      บ
 บ  come in and bitch at us, it makes us want to rip you some more.  Ok       บ
 บ  enough of this.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, this is for the people that come in and say "SEND ME THE NEWEST  บ
 บ  RCN!"  You don't have to beg!!!!  Before you nag people for it try this.  บ
 บ  Look in the channel for someone named *dcc (anythingdcc).  If they exist  บ
 บ  type this : "/MSG <nick> xdcc list"  If they list that they have it type  บ
 บ  this : "/MSG <nick> xdcc send #<pack@>"                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      OK!!  NOW, if there isn't a DCC in the channel look at the topic.     บ
 บ  It will usually have an FTP or Web page adrress!  If they aren't there,   บ
 บ  then ask.  Please don't just come in and BEG. It is very unbecoming.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Also, for people that want to write for RCN, you don't have to ask    บ
 บ  for an RCN app.  Just write something and send it to me.  If it is good   บ
 บ  we use it, if not, well.. we don't.  However, our editors are very        บ
 บ  patient and they will try to unscramble any submission, regardless of     บ
 บ  your English skills.  Also, we readily accept submissions written in      บ
 บ  French, Hebrew, Spanish, or Swedish.  Don't worry, we'll get it           บ
 บ  translated!  (Of course, we still prefer English!)  If you can keep       บ
 บ  submitting to RCN you will become a member.  But don't ask what the       บ
 บ  topic should be, if we had all the topics we could write the whole        บ
 บ  magazine, the topics are the hard part!                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

    ฿฿฿฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿             ฿฿฿ฐ฿ฐ     ฿
                ฿฿฿฿        ฿  e d i t o r i a l !  ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I've been around for nearly three years now.  No, I have never been   บ
 บ  "elite k-rad kick-ass d00d," but I did run a small warez board for        บ
 บ  around 2 years.  I recently closed it so I could play games (har har      บ
 บ  har).  The only good games I've played recently are of course, games      บ
 บ  like Duke3D, Quake, etc.  But my best memories are with those games from  บ
 บ  '93 and such.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What is it with game programmers, these days?  They seem to enjoy     บ
 บ  taking a camera, walking down the block, burning the film on a CD,        บ
 บ  adding a keyboard handler, package.  Oh sure, I would probably do the     บ
 บ  same thing if I wanted to make money.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And that's what you get: 50, 60 even over 70 disks.  Most of the      บ
 บ  time, and I'm sure a lot of you will agree on this, there's no more than  บ
 บ  2 disks of actual programming/playable shit.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Really, the size is relevant of only one factor.  How good is the     บ
 บ  intro?  How many times did you start a game, look at the intro for about  บ
 บ  5 minutes while drooling all over your crotch to find out the game is a   บ
 บ  VGA, 16 color piece of junk?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Spock                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Spock,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After extensive research over a long period of time by a top-notch    บ
 บ  team of scientists, we have come to the conclusion that, no, playing the  บ
 บ  Space Invaders game under the influence of narcotics does NOT cause       บ
 บ  breast cancer.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Vulcan Officer Aboard     บ
 บ                                                  USS Marijuana             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Xenon,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, Xenon!  How are you?  I've been trying to reach you, but it     บ

 บ  Dear Anonymous,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      At your UNIX prompt type "man chmod" -- that will load up the manual  บ
 บ  to the CHMOD command.  There are too many options to list and it would    บ
 บ  be much better for your comprehension of the chmod program to load up     บ
 บ  the manual for it.  By the way, the "man" command can be initiated on     บ
 บ  any other command to get information about it.  Hmm... wonder if you can  บ
 บ  do "man man!" Off to check...                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Waynekerr                 บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It has been called to my attention, that the local boards that I      บ
 บ  used to call were going under.  I know most of this it true due to the    บ
 บ  fact that we now have 3 Internet service providers in our area local to   บ
 บ  everyone.  I was told that before the Internet came around there were 30  บ
 บ  boards local where I live.  Now there are 5.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All the boards died within one year of when the Internet came to my   บ
 บ  town.  Now, I know for some people that they used to like calling local   บ
 บ  boards and playing Legend of the Red Dragon and other games like that     บ
 บ  but now it's to the point it you want to have a decent board you need to  บ
 บ  run it on the Internet to get calls.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I predict by the year 2000 the way it is going now there will be      บ
 บ  very FEW local boards in your area, like I know mine.  I used to run      บ
 บ  one.  I took it down and now am setup for the Internet I just need my     บ
 บ  static IP connection.  And I am off on my journey to the great beyond of  บ
 บ  the Internet.  And what do most people want when they telnet to a board?  บ
 บ  Warez mostly.  I don't know too many people who don't run a board and     บ
 บ  don't have them.  It's just an everyday occurrence now.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      With the major groups like DOD (Drink or Die) and PWA (Pirates with   บ
 บ  Attitudes) releasing the AWSOME software they get, it's just too big.     บ
 บ  But if you want to run a thriving board, you need a few things.           บ
 บ  Internet, Warez, people who call, and cool ansi's from ACiD (Ansi         บ
 บ  Creators in Demand) or another group like that.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Bass Extream              บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Rom Racer            บ
 บ    Subject  : Razor 666?                Affiliation : RZR Coordinator      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Razor 1911 has been one of the top groups in the scene for many     บ
 บ        years now, and many would consider it the best group of all time,   บ
 บ        however, there are some that would say that Razor 1911 is a dying   บ
 บ        group, and that Prestige is the new king of the hill, do you        บ
 บ        believe that is true?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: I would not say that Razor 1911 is dying, perhaps we are not in     บ
 บ        our prime. But, we are certainly still alive.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you believe that Prestige has taken Razor 1911's place in the    บ
 บ        games scene as the #1 group?  Razor 1911 has definitely not         บ
 บ        released as MANY games as Prestige, but the games that Razor 1911   บ
 บ        has released, such as WarCraft 2 (14 Disks with the Expansion       บ
 บ        Set), are usually better cracked and have a high chance of          บ
 บ        working.  Do you believe that Prestige releases also have a high    บ
 บ        rate of working?                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: Razor 1911 has been known for many years to release quality         บ
 บ        working titles.  Now, all groups come and go, but Razor 1911 will   บ
 บ        always be around.  Prestige does not have the same long term        บ
 บ        reputation as Razor 1911 does.  I cannot say how long Prestige      บ
 บ        will be able to continue with their high volume of releases, in     บ
 บ        most cases equal to Razor 1911 standards.  Then again, Prestige     บ
 บ        has messed up a few recently, but that is expected from a new       บ
 บ        group.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What are these mess ups by Prestige that could have come about      บ
 บ        because of their young age?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: For example, Prestige's release of Frank Thomas Baseball did not    บ
 บ        allow pitching.  Miscellaneous bugs as such in their releases,      บ
 บ        which can really happen to anyone, unless you have the              บ
 บ        organization and experience to have things tested properly, are     บ
 บ        not necessarily due to their young age.  But because of their       บ
 บ        young age, they most likely haven't had the time to setup a         บ
 บ        clockwork-like system of getting their releases out smoothly.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What is this clockwork-like system that you are describing? And     บ
 บ        how can other games groups learn from Razor 1911's experience?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: Well for example, Razor 1911 has a good reputation for releases     บ
 บ        working properly that are properly cracked.  However certain        บ
 บ        groups (in some cases based out of 718), do not have such a good    บ
 บ        reputation for things working properly, I am sure if the group in   บ
 บ        question (I would rather not mention any names at this point),      บ
 บ        would schedule in the time to test a release to make sure that the  บ
 บ        crack is fully working, a lot of problems could have been avoided.  บ
 บ        There is really nothing to be learned from Razor 1911's             บ
 บ        experience.  Experience itself is the key.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: A good release is guaranteed to be spread to many people, but even  บ
 บ        Razor 1911 has to release some games here and there that are just   บ
 บ        not fun.  It's not Razor 1911's fault, it's just that some          บ
 บ        companies can't program fun games.  And when that happens, how      บ
 บ        does the courier section of Razor 1911 help spread its releases to  บ
 บ        the masses even when the game just does not want to spread?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: Obviously in a games group situation, priority goes to the boards.  บ
 บ        Once a release has been put on our HQ boards, we then take it over  บ
 บ        to the Internet by procedure.  Once a release is on all of the      บ
 บ        main distribution points, there is really nothing we can do to      บ
 บ        force the end user to download it.  It is not our responsibility    บ
 บ        to market it.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How do you take it over to the Internet by procedure?  What do you  บ
 บ        mean by "procedure?"  Also, what are the requirements for a board   บ
 บ        that wants to become affiliated with Razor 1911.  And when a board  บ
 บ        does become affiliated, how does one become more than a member      บ
 บ        board to become a HQ board?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: By procedure, I mean it is how things are normally done, sort of    บ
 บ        "by the book."  The requirements of a board that would like to      บ
 บ        become a part of Razor 1911 are normally evaluated on an            บ
 บ        individual basis.  We look for boards in which the sysop is able    บ
 บ        to actively contribute to the group.  Generally, I would assume, I  บ
 บ        have not been in Razor 1911 at the time an HQ board was appointed,  บ
 บ        that a HQ board would be selected on the basis of hardware, nodes,  บ
 บ        traffic, and of course the sysops level of contribution.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: On the note of experience that you mentioned earlier, what          บ
 บ        surprises me is that many of the Prestige leaders such as The       บ
 บ        Renegade Chemist and Zeus, were former leaders of Razor 1911        บ
 บ        during its peak.  Why wouldn't they be showing the experience that  บ
 บ        they have acquired over the years in making sure that Prestige      บ
 บ        releases work in a more timely fashion?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: In a new group environment, having established people, such as The  บ
 บ        Renegade Chemist and Zeus is always a plus, but it cannot totally   บ
 บ        evade the problems which arise in a new group.  You must keep in    บ
 บ        mind that a group is a group, a team effort I should say.  You      บ
 บ        cannot base a group on the merits of a few strong individuals.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I do find it interesting that many Razor 1911 couriers are also     บ
 บ        couriers in Rapier.  Why is that so?  Is Rapier official couriers   บ
 บ        for Razor 1911?  For example, on Street Spyders, the Razor 1911     บ
 บ        WHQ which also happens to be one of the fastest boards in the       บ
 บ        world, most of the top uploaders are usually members of Rapier and  บ
 บ        Razor 1911.  Perhaps there is a team effort here?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: It is purely coincidence that many Rapier couriers are also Razor   บ
 บ        1911 couriers.  Both Rapier and Razor 1911 only take the best,      บ
 บ        therefore, it is likely that both groups will have a similar        บ
 บ        member base.  It also happens to be that Street Spyders is the      บ
 บ        Rapier US HQ and also being the Razor WHQ.  Rapier obviously wants  บ
 บ        the best boards, and so does Razor 1911, therefore it is likely     บ
 บ        that their choices would overlap.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I heard rumors that Rapier might have disbanded earlier this week,  บ
 บ        or that perhaps many Rapier members left Rapier for Everlast        บ
 บ        because you did not have enough time to run the group, is there     บ
 บ        any truth to that?  Is Rapier still alive?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: I cannot comment on Rapiers current status.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Ever since my friends brought me into the scene, I've always asked  บ
 บ        myself, "What does the 1911 in Razor 1911 mean?"  Nobody has ever   บ
 บ        been able to tell me, but I do hope that you will be able to        บ
 บ        answer that question.  And please do, or I will have to kill you.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: 777h.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: 777h?  What does that mean?  I will kill you if you don't tell me.  บ
 บ        Is 1911 some kind of Satanic thing?  Like, you take 1911 and you    บ
 บ        some how rearrange the numbers, and then you multiply and subtract  บ
 บ        them in some strange fashion, and you get 666?  Like that Ozzy      บ
 บ        Osbourne music video, where his forehead has a 9454 print, and      บ
 บ        it's actually some sort of allusion to the printmark of the Beast   บ
 บ        (Anti-Christ) found in the Bible?  See, I was bored, so I tossed    บ
 บ        9454 in my head, and if you multiply 9 times 4, you get 36.  Now    บ
 บ        if you add 5 plus 4, you get 9, so now you're left with 369.  So    บ
 บ        if you take 3 from 9 and add that 3 to the first 3, you get 666.    บ
 บ        This can be confusing, but you get the point.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: I suppose we will leave that as a mystery.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Bummer.  Oh well, you can't win them all.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

  ฿฿฿ฐ฿฿     ฿     ฿                       ฿฿฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Bug Lord & Morphine  บ
 บ    Subject  : Napalm Cheats Again?      Affiliation : Epic Leaders         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What kind of group is Epic?  It's fairly new, but I've seen its     บ
 บ        releases around many fast sites this past week.  How did Epic       บ
 บ        start?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ BUG: Well, it's a games releasing group.  It was started when Morphine   บ
 บ        and I decided that when we were in ROR (Release on Rampage), our    บ
 บ        work was being wasted.  Morphine's supplies were being done by      บ
 บ        Prestige first, and my couriering was pointless for a release       บ
 บ        group that did only did 1 game each month.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What did you mean when you said that Morphine's supplies were       บ
 บ        being done by Prestige first?  Was Morphine part of Prestige?  I    บ
 บ        thought you said that both of you were members of ROR?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ MOR: No, well all of the releases I obtained took ROR too long to get    บ
 บ        out and they never got the releases it out it was getting on my     บ
 บ        nerves so we decided to start up Epic so that we could make sure    บ
 บ        that that crap didn't happen to me and other suppliers.  I don't    บ
 บ        want to sound like I'm dissing ROR, but the records do show that    บ
 บ        ROR released very FEW games.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Morphine, when you supplied for ROR, why did it take them so long   บ
 บ        to release something?  Were they busy checking to make sure that    บ
 บ        the game was fully cracked and working?  If so, then ROR's          บ
 บ        precaution would actually be good for the scene.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ MOR: Well, it just seemed that the people that they needed were never    บ
 บ        around to do their job to get the releases out.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: In a way then, Epic is a split off of ROR?  Now that Epic is here,  บ
 บ        what distinguishes it from other release groups?  What makes it     บ
 บ        special?  Why is it not just ANOTHER lame one week games group?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ BUG: Well, only the leadership of Epic split off of ROR, and even then   บ
 บ        we don't think of it like that.  ROR was simply the group that      บ
 บ        both Morphine and I were in at one point in time.  We don't really  บ
 บ        consider ourselves special, we just get the job done and will       บ
 บ        continue to do so.  You should also know that Morphine and I were   บ
 บ        away from the scene for a while before this, so we were only in     บ
 บ        ROR a few weeks.  I'm not saying that ROR is bad, but we really     บ
 บ        don't have anything to do with them anymore.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Specify what you meant when you said, "We don't really consider     บ
 บ        ourselves special, we just get the job done and will continue to    บ
 บ        do so."  What are you guys doing that you will contine to do, but   บ
 บ        that does not make Epic special?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ MOR: Well, Epic is no different than any other games group which has     บ
 บ        succeeded except that we are doing so in a smaller scale.  We get   บ
 บ        our releases and we get them cracked and we get them out to the     บ
 บ        sites.  That's how the scene is, you don't need to be special to    บ
 บ        do that, you just need to be organized.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: While running Epic, have you encountered any problems?  I have      บ
 บ        heard rumors that the release of Gender Wars was supposed to be     บ
 บ        released by Epic, but the release was then stolen by Prophet, the   บ
 บ        leader of Napalm, is that true?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ BUG: Well, we like to give everyone the benefit of the doubt, and if     บ
 บ        Prophet did it by accident, then we can forgive that, but there is  บ
 บ        a little bit of doubt.  We had placed our release on the Internet   บ
 บ        shell account of X-Factor, a Legion leader, while waiting for a     บ
 บ        cracker to get it.  It seems that somehow Dark Force found the      บ
 บ        release on the shell (it's also a Legion release site), and gave    บ
 บ        it to Prophet.  Prophet then uploaded it to Pentium Domination.     บ
 บ        It could be an innocent mistake.  We also got conflicting answers   บ
 บ        by Prophet when he was questioned, and he never did admit to it.    บ
 บ        But tracing the path of the spread clearly leads back to Pentium    บ
 บ        Domination where it was uploaded by Prophet.  We missed the final   บ
 บ        release of Gender Wars to Razor 1911 by only a few minutes, and if  บ
 บ        now for this extreme distraction we would probably have had the     บ
 บ        release.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You lost the release to Razor 1911?  Did Napalm actually ever       บ
 บ        release the Gender Wars stolen from Epic?  Prophet is known for     บ
 บ        stealing cracks and releases from other games groups, but did he    บ
 บ        actually do anything with the stolen release this time?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ BUG: No, which points to the fact that it could have been an accident,   บ
 บ        and they didn't know it was uncracked.  However, there is always    บ
 บ        the possibility that Napalm WAS cracking the Epic release and       บ
 บ        simply didn't do it in time.  The conflicting answers from Prophet  บ
 บ        don't make it seem any more likely to be the first.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: On the note of another release, NHL PowerPlay, which was released   บ
 บ        by Coredump, but unfortunately, the game was knowingly released     บ
 บ        without a crack.  I later noticed that Epic released NHL PowerPlay  บ
 บ        as well, is the Epic version any different from Coredump's          บ
 บ        careless release, or was the Epic release of NHL PowerPlay also     บ
 บ        uncracked?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ BUG: No, it was not a dupe.  It was one of the best possible releases    บ
 บ        for a new group such as Epic.  Coredump knowing that it was not     บ
 บ        cracked, released it uncracked, and it was nuked everywhere, which  บ
 บ        led to the humiliating fact that many members of Coredump started   บ
 บ        denying the fact that they were even in the group.  Razor 1911      บ
 บ        declared that the game was uncrackable, and Holy Beast from         บ
 บ        Prestige tried to crack it but failed.  However, Misha, the god of  บ
 บ        cracking, cracked the game for Epic.  To help out the people who    บ
 บ        can't follow directions from the NFO, you must do a CUSTOM install  บ
 บ        and then you must do a select all.  That should keep the channel    บ
 บ        #Epic free from being flooded by lamers, wait, calling stupid       บ
 บ        people "lamers" is politically incorrect, I actually meant "people  บ
 บ        with low intelligence" or rather, "the installationally             บ
 บ        challenged."                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Has Coredump shown any resentment toward Epic?  After all, Epic     บ
 บ        did make Coredump look really lame.  Yes, and I do call them lame.  บ
 บ        I don't like being politically correct, so sue me.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ BUG: Well, Incarnate and Perfect Form have been the only ones to give    บ
 บ        us any problems.  They tried to get NHL PowerPlay cracked like 5    บ
 บ        days after we released our working version, but they still          บ
 บ        couldn't get it cracked so they got really mad and started telling  บ
 บ        every one how the Epic version of NHL PowerPlay didn't even work    บ
 บ        when everyone who downloaded it would know that it does work.  I    บ
 บ        think that most Epic members are still banned from channel #CD      บ
 บ        (Coredump's IRC channel), and a few of Coredump members did try to  บ
 บ        infiltrate Epic, rather pathetically too since we knew that the     บ
 บ        Coredump spies were discussing "tricking Epic."  I believe there    บ
 บ        were a couple threats, and tKLP informed us that Incarnate was      บ
 บ        trying to steal our crack for their release.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ        infiltrate us?"                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ BUG: Someone named Pioneer tried a "I really hate Coredump, I want to    บ
 บ        join Epic," but we have our own spies in channel #CD and we were    บ
 บ        totally aware of their pathetic attempts at infiltrating Epic.      บ
 บ        Some other members of Coredump tried as well, but Pioneer was       บ
 บ        their best actor.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Dam, with spies and all, I'm surprised they're not Communist or     บ

 บ    Reporter : Crack                     Interviewee : Charley              บ
 บ    Subject  : Small Group+Big Ego=CB4?  Affiliation : CB4 Leader           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What kind of group is CB4 (Cellblock 4)?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: First of all, I would like to tell you who I am.  Like 8 months     บ
 บ        ago, my ex-boyfriend (and YES, I am a girl) introduced me to some   บ
 บ        of the members of oG (The Original Gangsters Syndicate, a little    บ
 บ        Swedish group).  I started supplying for them.  Later on, I         บ
 บ        established contact with Ivanhoe (now one of the leaders of CB4)    บ
 บ        and some of the other members of the old Rebels.  When they left    บ
 บ        Rebels and started CB4, they convinced me to join them as a leader  บ
 บ        of the group.  CB4 is a release group.  Our goal is to crack and    บ
 บ        release all that we can get our hands on and to have FUN!!!         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: When you mentioned "the old Rebels," to what were you referring     บ
 บ        to?                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Some of the old members of Rebels left Rebels to help start CB4.    บ
 บ        Leatherman, who was a former leader in Rebels, started CB4 near     บ
 บ        the end of 1995 with only a few crackers.  In the beginning of      บ
 บ        1996, 2 more Rebels members, Ivanhoe and Mercury, joined his        บ
 บ        efforts.  In February, CB4 merged with oG, where some of my         บ
 บ        seniors and I joined CB4, and that's when CB4 became a real group,  บ
 บ        and not just one of the small groups.  Later on, Leatherman left    บ
 บ        the group due to personal problems and after a short while,         บ
 บ        Imposter joined CB4 as a leader.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you consider your group, CB4, a top notch releasing group?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Well, we want to stay a small group, with only 1 or 2 member sites  บ
 บ        and no boards or couriers.  Sure, a small group can have problems   บ
 บ        as well, but it's easier to keep the group together when everyone   บ
 บ        knows each other.  That makes it easier to work together as a       บ
 บ        team.  All our members are 100% loyal to the group, and you know,   บ
 บ        you don't have to be big in size to be a great release group!       บ
 บ        Sometimes, when things are going really well with the releasing     บ
 บ        and stuff, it's easy to develop a big ego.  But in a small group    บ
 บ        like ours, there is always someone there to pull you down from the  บ
 บ        skies again.  To be honest with you, it is more important that our  บ
 บ        members have the right personality, than that they can supply like  บ
 บ        7 releases a week.  The most important thing for us is to have      บ
 บ        fun, and we like the laid back attitude towards the scene.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Has CB4 ever released warez before other release groups?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Yes, we have released like 10 to 20 releases a week in the last     บ
 บ        couple of weeks.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Does CB4 specialize in releasing games, or utils, or both?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: We only release utils.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Would you say that CB4 ranks up with other utils groups such as     บ
 บ        Mortality?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Yeah, sure, we are kicking the scene right now and we have lots     บ
 บ        and lots of releases, but as I said before, the most important      บ
 บ        thing for us is to have fun and we are not competing with anyone.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Please tell us what having fun in your group is like.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Well, we all do it because it's a nice way of breaking the law,     บ
 บ        hehe, no.  It's fun to see how far you can go with a small group    บ
 บ        like ours.  Many other BIG groups wants to merge with us, but we    บ
 บ        want to keep the group small so that we don't HAVE to do things in  บ
 บ        any other way but our own CB4 way.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How long has CB4 been around in the scene?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Eh, Leatherman started the group in 1995 and we have been           บ
 บ        releasing like 10 to 20 releases a week since February.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Where do you guys get so many releases?  How do CB4 suppliers       บ
 บ        obtain their software?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: No, now I'm lying to you.  In February and March, we had like       บ
 บ        20-30 releases a month.  Hey, never tell anyone how our suppliers   บ
 บ        get their hands on the software!  Rule #1!!!                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Let me take a wild guess, are they beta testers?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Bwhahahhaha, I won't tell you!!!                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You've made your point abundantly clear that CB4 is a small group,  บ
 บ        but it is probably receiving plenty of applications each week.      บ
 บ        For those who might be interested, how are applicants selected to   บ
 บ        be given membership in CB4?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Like I said before, the most important thing for us when we look    บ
 บ        at applicants is not whether or not they can supply thousands of    บ
 บ        releases, but their personality.  We want to keep the group small,  บ
 บ        so I guess it's hard to join us.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I have asked many people about CB4, it seems that no one has ever   บ
 บ        heard of the group (including me), you said CB4 was very good and   บ
 บ        that it released 10 to 20 releases a week, and yet, nobody knows    บ
 บ        about the group, how can that be?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: Well, perhaps they don't read RCN!?  Or perhaps you've been asking  บ
 บ        the wrong people?  Nah, but we are a small group and we don't make  บ
 บ        much noise.  Our releases are on all the big sites and you have     บ
 บ        them in your weekly warez list, so I don't know why people haven't  บ
 บ        heard about us.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You mentioned earlier that some other groups wanted to merge with   บ
 บ        CB4, can you name some?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CB4: No, I don't want to do that.  I don't know if the other groups      บ
 บ        would like that, but I can tell you this, those groups that asked   บ
 บ        us are the biggest in the scene.  :)                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ RCN: I've been informed that tHA is one of the largest internet          บ

 บ        address and grabbed our channel, which makes our people pissed off  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Samuraion            บ
 บ    Subject  : Bad+Bad=Good?             Affiliation : Legion Council       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Many know that Legion started a few weeks ago, and has shown its    บ
 บ        presence in the utils scene as a group with a lot of potential.  I  บ
 บ        am aware that Legion came about as a merge, but which groups        บ
 บ        merged to form Legion?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: Basically, Legion was a merge between Siva and Logistix, but 000    บ
 บ        (former leader of Dawn/Fierce) also brought along some of their     บ
 บ        members after it died, and so what Legion really is, is the best    บ
 บ        of Dawn, Logistix, and Siva.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: The best of Dawn, Logistix, and Siva?  From what I know, none of    บ
 บ        the 3 groups had any real quality and reputation.  How has          บ
 บ        bringing the best of the 3 groups formed a better and more          บ
 บ        respectable group, Legion?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: What we really did was cut a lot of members down.  We took all our  บ
 บ        suppliers (respectively), and some other important members, and     บ
 บ        created a new group with 3 times the suppliers, and we are all      บ
 บ        very dedicated and working toward being a competition to the more   บ
 บ        respectable utils releasing groups.  And we all treat each other    บ
 บ        with respect, work together, and that is what really brings a good  บ
 บ        group together.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I am aware that Judge Dredd was the leader of Dawn, but I do not    บ
 บ        see him as a part of Legion?  Was he taken out of Legion because    บ
 บ        he was dead weight?  Or did Legion merely take the suppliers out    บ
 บ        of Dawn and left all other members of Dawn to themselves?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: Well, Dawn wasn't really considered a part of the merge I think.    บ
 บ        This is because 000 came to Legion after Logistix and Siva had      บ
 บ        already merged for a few days, but as for Judge Dredd, I haven't    บ
 บ        seen him for a long time, and I think he's with a courier group     บ
 บ        right now.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Were there any problems that resulted when the merge did take       บ
 บ        place?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: What we really needed was some organization at first, but after a   บ
 บ        little while, everything went well, and we had our releases going.  บ
 บ        However, since we had some top couriers in the group, they were     บ
 บ        all arguing about who gets to spread the releases to which sites.   บ
 บ        That was bothering us for a few days, but in the end, we got it     บ
 บ        all settled down, and everything went smoothly from there on.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Which top couriers argued about where the releases should be        บ
 บ        spread, and how did everything eventually settle down?  Did you     บ
 บ        just tell all your couriers to stop arguing, or did you have to     บ
 บ        threaten to kick them out of Legion before they would listen?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: I would rather not reveal their names, but we have thought about    บ
 บ        it for a while, and have asked a few of them to resign or upload    บ
 บ        to another site.  But in the end, everything worked out alright,    บ
 บ        no conflicts, nothing.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Many young utils groups, and by far, Legion is not an exception,    บ
 บ        go through troubles when they first release.  Nearly all young      บ
 บ        utils groups go through troubles of releasing utils that are        บ
 บ        broken or are dupes.  How has Legion answered to those that accuse  บ
 บ        it of releasing warez that are broken and on several occasions,     บ
 บ        releases that are dupes?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: I have no comment, but I do believe that we have not duped on any   บ
 บ        release.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you believe that there might be any egos within the group?  For  บ
 บ        example, a few days ago, when I joined channel #Legion, I was       บ
 บ        threatened of being banned from #Legion by X-Factor, Legion         บ
 บ        Council, simply because I was joining the channel to look for a     บ
 บ        friend, and when I couldn't find my friend, I left the channel.     บ
 บ        He got extremely mad at me and started yelling at me because I      บ
 บ        joined and then left the channel.  Do you believe that attitudes    บ
 บ        as such might be hurting the group?  After all, nobody likes        บ
 บ        working with stuckup egos.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: Well, X-Factor is an exception. I've known him for a while, he's    บ
 บ        special.  He just about pissed off everyone in the group,           บ
 บ        including me, but he's a nice guy if you know him.  But as for the  บ
 บ        egos, there have been no egos in the group, and if there ever will  บ
 บ        be, it will be dealt with seriously.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: In your opinion, how does Legion stand among the better utils       บ
 บ        groups such as PWA (Pirated with Attitudes) and Rebels?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: We are still new at this, but our members all have experience, and  บ
 บ        we are still in the process of organization, but once everything    บ
 บ        is settled, we will be a competition to them.  We got all the       บ
 บ        suppliers we need, and all we need now is time, time to build up    บ
 บ        our name so we can stand up there with some of the other stronger   บ
 บ        utils groups.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You mentioned earlier that there were conflicts between different   บ
 บ        top couriers within Legion.  Has that hindered Legion's ability in  บ
 บ        seeking after an official courier group to courier Legion           บ
 บ        releases?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: About official couriers, we had a lot of thought on that.  But we   บ
 บ        do have a strong Internet team, and we are on all the top sites of  บ
 บ        the world, so couriering shouldn't be a problem.  However, we did   บ
 บ        consider Empire as our official couriers, but the                   บ
 บ        negotiations/terms came out differently from what we discussed, so  บ
 บ        we decided to go with Malice at the moment.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What were these negotiations/terms that were not met by Empire?     บ
 บ        Did Empire not live up to their word?  Or perhaps Legion was        บ
 บ        simply more interested in being affiliated with Malice because it   บ
 บ        is an older group and is more well known?                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGN: Well, Empire did not meet the terms that one of their staff said,   บ
 บ        because it seemed that their staff have different points of view.   บ
 บ        We had a great offer from Empire, and after it was all settled,     บ
 บ        another Empire staff gave us a different story.  And since a few    บ
 บ        of the Legion Council are also members of Malice, and Malice is an  บ
 บ        older group with a lot more experience, and had an even better      บ
 บ        offer, it makes sense to have them spread our releases.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Byron Zed            บ
 บ    Subject  : fATE Lacks Support?       Affiliation : WWR High Membership  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: WWR (World Wide Releasing) never ceases to amaze me.  It's one of   บ
 บ        those small groups that have been around for a long time, but has   บ
 บ        yet to change much.  How is that so?  And for those who don't know  บ
 บ        much about WWR, what kind of release group is WWR?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Well, WWR has gotten itself a big reputation on a local level, but  บ
 บ        not so much on the Internet.  WWR is a releasing group, and it      บ
 บ        releases utils.  I guess we didn't got the right people for doing   บ
 บ        the right stuff.  We had fATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange)          บ
 บ        couriering for us, but that didn't help much either.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Why has it gained respect only on a local level?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: As I said, we didn't had the right people to do the couriering      บ
 บ        stuff, and localy it was more easier for our own couriers to move   บ
 บ        WWR releases from board to board without calling long distance or   บ
 บ        phreaking for it.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Certainly, fATE could only help WWR spread warez in as much as WWR  บ
 บ        can release, and in that, I have yet to see much, so the fault was  บ
 บ        not with fATE, but with WWR.  What did you expect fATE to do for    บ
 บ        WWR that would have helped the group?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Well, first, fATE was coming to me with their offer, to courier     บ
 บ        for WWR.  I of course said yes and told the other high membership   บ
 บ        about it.  It wasn't what I expected it to be.  I thought they      บ
 บ        would courier NOT only to their sites, but IRC offers and BBS       บ
 บ        also, and I thought that they would support WWR's boards as well.   บ
 บ        I guess I was wrong.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Most utils groups have seniors that are based in the U.S., but      บ
 บ        I've been informed that most WWR seniors live in Europe, is that    บ
 บ        true?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Yes, we have two seniors that live in the U.S., and two that live   บ
 บ        in Europe.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What are some of WWR's quality releases in the recent weeks?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Some of WWR's best releases include Visual Basic v4.2, Delphi       บ
 บ        v2.1, Romworks, Access Developer v7.0, and Paint Shop Pro v4.0.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: After WWR left fATE, did WWR seek out for another courier group     บ
 บ        that could satisfy its needs?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Well, that "leave" happened only 2 days ago, so for now, I don't    บ
 บ        know where to go, there is Malice, RTS (Request to Send), RiSC      บ
 บ        (Rise in Superior Couriering), and others.  I'm just waiting for    บ
 บ        the right courier group to show up that will help WWR out in        บ
 บ        couriering.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What makes you think that any of the above mentioned courier        บ
 บ        groups would want to be official couriers for WWR?  What would you  บ
 บ        offer them?  You could offer them releases, and you named some      บ
 บ        good ones just a few minutes ago, but many of them were dupes and   บ
 บ        were thus nuked off all the major boards.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: ALL of them?  Well, I can't really tell now what I have to offer.   บ
 บ        If they'll throw an offer or demand at me, I'll try to fulfill it   บ
 บ        and go with it.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What makes WWR different from other utils groups?  There are tons   บ
 บ        out there and WWR might just be a dime a dozen.  What makes it      บ
 บ        better than other utils groups, or perhaps, it's not?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Well, I didn't say we're better than anyone out there.  It's just   บ
 บ        that there are TONS of utils coming out everyday in the stores,     บ
 บ        and not all the groups can release those utils.  So I try to fill   บ
 บ        in the missing spot of those utils and release them.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: "... there are TONS of utils coming out everyday in the stores,     บ
 บ        and not all the groups can release those utils," what do you mean   บ
 บ        by that?  Why can't other utils groups release what WWR releases?   บ
 บ        Are WWR releases of low quality, and thus, other utils groups       บ
 บ        refuse to release them?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Well, some suppliers go to the store and bring whatever there is,   บ
 บ        and sometimes they miss one or two things.  So here are two good    บ
 บ        utils to worth releasing, and woops, no one got it.  So I try to    บ
 บ        grab it, and release it.  I also forgot to mention that we don't    บ
 บ        release any shitty util that comes out, we try to release only the  บ
 บ        utils that people will ACTUALLY use for their needs.  We don't      บ
 บ        release those shitty screen savers that people are juming just to   บ
 บ        release it.  You saw some of the titles I said, and you saw those   บ
 บ        are requested utils, so we release them.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: There is one problem though, I just went through a dupe check list  บ
 บ        on BBX, a very fast RiSC site, and none of those files you          บ
 บ        mentioned are on there released under WWR.  I also received word    บ
 บ        that the WWR releases you mentioned are not on there because they   บ
 บ        were nuked for being fakes or dupes, why is that?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: Dupes?  You saw any where else that someone released those?  And I  บ
 บ        can't prove you that those were fakes.  The only thing that you     บ
 บ        could do to check them, is to download them yourself and see for    บ
 บ        yourself.  Maybe it's not on the sites because we've just started   บ
 บ        then and we were local.  Maybe someone told the siteops to nuke     บ
 บ        them because they were "dupes" and "fakes" and the siteops without  บ
 บ        checking it, just nuked it.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: That is very possible, how long has WWR been around on the          บ
 บ        Internet?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ WWR: We've been on the internet for about 3 to 4 months, and we've been  บ
 บ        around in the scene for about 7+ months total.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Judge Dredd          บ
 บ    Subject  : Another Dead Merge?       Affiliation : Dawn President       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What was your position in the late Dawn, and what were your duties  บ
 บ        for that group?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: I was the founder and the leader of Dawn team since October of      บ
 บ        1995.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I know that Dawn the games group died in 1995 when it tried to      บ
 บ        merge into Legacy, another games group of which I was a part of,    บ
 บ        but I also know that Dawn the utils group was later revived in      บ
 บ        1996 and became quite prominent, yet once again, it has died, why   บ
 บ        is that so?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: We started out as a game group back then, releasing some exellent   บ
 บ        games, but then somewhere in the beginning of 1996 we decided to    บ
 บ        release both games and utilities.  Then I decided to stay with      บ
 บ        utils and when Tyranny came back I went to them and Dawn became a   บ
 บ        utils only group.  We had released some pretty good stuff then,     บ
 บ        and was offered a lot of merges, but I I had bad expierence with    บ
 บ        merges, plus they were all in-merges meaning that Dawn was losing   บ
 บ        its name, until Fierce team came along.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What happened when to Dawn when the Fierce team came along?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: They were releasing very legit utilities back then, and they        บ
 บ        agreed to keep the name Dawn, and I thought to myself that in that  บ
 บ        time things couldn't be better, Dawn in RCN's weekly utils review   บ
 บ        in one of the weeks finished 2nd after PWA and now had more power,  บ
 บ        but I was wrong.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I do remember that Dawn finished 2nd in the utils review, and that  บ
 บ        is very good for a new utils group.  Dawn had a very good week, so  บ
 บ        it only seemed natural to show them off to the masses, but you      บ
 บ        also mention, "but I was wrong."  How were you wrong, and when did  บ
 บ        you realize that you were wrong?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: When I had to take 2 week break because of personal reasons and I   บ
 บ        left group for Ebola and Darkrage.  I am not going to blame either  บ
 บ        fo them.  Ebola had recieved $1000 phone bill and Darkrage had      บ
 บ        family problems, Anyway, when I return there was a complete mess,   บ
 บ        the channel had about 50 people in fighting and bullshitting.  I    บ
 บ        just couldn't take it.  I kicked everyone out and I decided to      บ
 บ        keep all of the loyal Dawn members, most of which were also         บ
 บ        suppliers.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: So you kicked everyone out of your group that couldn't supply, but  บ
 บ        that still should not have killed Dawn.  As long as you had         บ
 บ        suppliers, you should have been able to keep Dawn releasing.  Why   บ
 บ        did Dawn eventually die then?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: We did not die.  We were looking for a nice place to merge.  We     บ
 บ        had the opportunities to merge into X-Force.  They're a great team  บ
 บ        but somehow when my people voted, they voted not to join them.      บ
 บ        Personally, I loved that opportunity, but I always consider the     บ
 บ        opinions of our people.  They wanted to go with Mortality, and I    บ
 บ        even sent Cryptic Pain a small release, but he just didn't seem     บ
 บ        too trustful of me, nothing personal, but yesterday we found our    บ
 บ        place where we want to be.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What place is this?  Where did Dawn merge into?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: As of yesterday all Dawn members are getting ready for a complete   บ
 บ        team merging with Sodom and their great friendly team run by Tok    บ
 บ        and Jecksom.  I had been friends with both of them, and I think we  บ
 บ        can kick some real ass, they're already on top 5 no doubt!          บ
 บ        Together we can really kick it.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What are you talking about?  There is no way Sodom is not one of    บ
 บ        the top 5 utils groups.  It's not even in content, there are tons   บ
 บ        of other groups that are in much better views than they are.  I     บ
 บ        can easily find 5 other utils groups that easily outrank Sodom      บ
 บ        both in release power and reputation.  For example, I'm sure that   บ
 บ        DOD (Drink or Die) is better than Sodom.  I'm also sure that        บ
 บ        Mortality, PWA, Rebels, and X-Force are all better than etter than  บ
 บ        Sodom.  That makes 5 other utils groups.  Perhaps you merged Dawn   บ
 บ        into Sodom for alterior motives?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: No, I believe that Sodom has better potentials than anyone else     บ
 บ        right now. Just watch them.  There was no other reason for Dawn to  บ
 บ        merge into Sodom.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Yes, they do have the potential, but unachieved potential is        บ
 บ        useless.  Anyway, what position will you be taking once you are a   บ
 บ        part of Sodom?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: We're about to discuss it when Tok returns home from Moscow, but    บ
 บ        I'll have at least a council position.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Why do you think Cryptic Pain, Mortality President, was so          บ
 บ        cautious in having you supply him with releases.  Shouldn't he      บ
 บ        have been grateful if those releases were of quality?  Do you have  บ
 บ        any ideas why he would not trust you?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: Oh no, he was grateful, but I told him not to release it, because   บ
 บ        in return for Dawn helping Mortality, he had to go with our         บ
 บ        couriering group to help Dawn out.  After I sent him a release and  บ
 บ        asked him if he's ready to go with our couriering group he said he  บ
 บ        wasn't sure and I told him not to release util I gave him, I        บ
 บ        didn't trust him enough.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What did you give him to release?  Was it a quality util?  If it    บ
 บ        was, he would have jumped on the opportunity instead of jerking     บ
 บ        around with you right?  Also, which courier group did you ask him   บ
 บ        to go with?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: Oh, he wasn't jerking around.  It's just that he had another        บ
 บ        promise to someone else.  No, that was not a quality release, but   บ
 บ        it was very legit and useful 2 disk util.  Well, I don't think it   บ
 บ        matters now.  Actually, there is a big story with that, but it's a  บ
 บ        completely different story which has nothing to do with Cryptic     บ
 บ        Pain ofcourse.  He's a good leader and he made Mortality one of     บ
 บ        the best groups in the world in a short period of time, so          บ
 บ        whatever I said about me trusting him, it has nothing to do with    บ
 บ        his great abilities as a leader.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Also, you mentioned earlier, "... pretty good stuff then, and was   บ
 บ        offered a lot of merges, but I I had bad expierence with merges,    บ
 บ        plus they were all in-merges meaning that Dawn was losing its       บ
 บ        name."  Isn't Dawn's current merge into Sodom an in-merge?  Why     บ
 บ        aren't you more cautious of Sodom, I thought you said that you had  บ
 บ        bad experiences with merges?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ DWN: Yes, but this time I am not aiming to run a group.  I am going to   บ
 บ        meaning that earlier when there was a merge I consider myself       บ
 บ        being of the leader, but now I stayed in the warez scene but I'm    บ
 บ        also join tradinng scene - a scene of a real challange and risc,    บ
 บ        not just sitting and packaging releases.  Therefore you're now      บ
 บ        interviewing Dredd & Impact.  I now officially change my name from  บ
 บ        Judge Dredd to Dredd & Impact.  As for Sodom, I'll be doing         บ
 บ        everything I can to get it on top.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
