 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Ju-Jutsu             บ
 บ    Subject  : Make Up Your Mind!        Affiliation : fTP Leader           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What kind of courier group is fTP (Full Throttle Pirates)?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: Our intention was to courier mainly to sites belonging to fTP and   บ
 บ        some IRC couriering too.  We might start releasing as soon as we    บ
 บ        get us some suppliers.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: It is my understanding that your group is based in Finland, is      บ
 บ        that true?  If so, has that hindered fTP's ability in competing     บ
 บ        with American based courier groups?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: Well, I am from Finland and some of our members are from Finland    บ
 บ        too, but that doesn't mean that we couldn't compete with American   บ
 บ        groups.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What makes your courier group fTP different from any other courier  บ
 บ        group?  There are tons out there and many people might think that   บ
 บ        fTP is just another lame courier group, is that true?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: We aren't new to the scene, like some lame courier groups that      บ
 บ        were started by newbies.  We know what we are doing.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How long have you been in the scene and what previous experience    บ
 บ        do you have with running courier groups?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: I've been in the scene for over 4 years or so, and I've couriered   บ
 บ        for many good and lame courier groups.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Which courier groups might those be?  Which of them do you          บ
 บ        consider good, and which of them do you consider lame?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: Yes.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Could you be more specific?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: There were many.  Most of them were lame.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Five minutes ago, you said "I've couriered for many good and lame   บ
 บ        courier groups."  Which good courier groups have you couriered      บ
 บ        for?  Let me rephrase my question, which good courier groups have   บ
 บ        you been in?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: I've couriered for Insanity and Malice.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Why did you leave Malice?  It certainly does have a better          บ
 บ        reputation than fTP.  Did you leave Malice to pursue your own       บ
 บ        goals of running your own courier group?  It seems like everyone    บ
 บ        says they've been a part of Malice these days, I'll have to check   บ
 บ        with Dorian Hawkmoon.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: It was a long time ago, besides I wanted to put up my own group.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Many courier groups enjoy being official couriers for release       บ
 บ        groups.  Is fTP official couriers for any release groups?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: Yes.  We are official couriers for the NEW Legacy.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Has this NEW Legacy given fTP lots to courier?  Last I checked,     บ
 บ        they have yet to release anything.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: The new Legacy gave us nothing to courier so far.  Well, we are     บ
 บ        new and so is Legacy.  Or it's lame, I don't know.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What are your future plans for fTP?  How do you suppose to make it  บ
 บ        a better group than it is now?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: Of course!  We just started.  Our future plans are to start         บ
 บ        releasing as soon as we get some more suppliers.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: So you plan to make fTP a release group?  I thought fTP was a       บ
 บ        courier group?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: Yes.  Clone is the other leader.  We already got some suppliers.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Wait, if fTP is a release group, then why is fTP official couriers  บ
 บ        for Legacy?  You guys really ought to make up your minds.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: We started out as couriers, and our future plans are to become a    บ
 บ        releasing group.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you guys plan on releasing games and utils, or do you plan on    บ
 บ        specializing fTP releases to either games or utils?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ fTP: I have decided that we will be releasing both games and utils, but  บ
 บ        we have not yet decided.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : ROR is Dead?  I wish.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Here's a little log file of what happened in channel #Reflux.  I was  บ
 บ  about to celebrate when I found out that ROR (Release on Rampage) was     บ
 บ  finally dead, I mean, after all, don't we all hate downloading fake       บ
 บ  releases?  I'm tired of downloading something to find that the filedates  บ
 บ  to the games have been rigged so it wouldn't get nuked, and I'm tired of  บ
 บ  downloading beta games that have been hex edited to say that they're the  บ
 บ  final version of something they're not.  You might be confused as to why  บ
 บ  ROR and RLX (Reflux) might have something in common, but hopefully, the   บ
 บ  log file will help clear things up.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crack> Tklp, is ROR dead?  Is Reflux the new ROR?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Tklp> Yes!!  Duh!!!  ROR is now Reflux, but keep it quiet until we       บ
 บ         debut.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Crack> Tklp, when are you going to tell everyone?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Tklp> When we do our first release.  Warhammer, make us a file_id.diz    บ
 บ         and give me the script.  I thought you wanted to join.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Warhammer> Fucking hell man, when you want something, you gotta have     บ
 บ              it.  Ok, hold on, I'll do one right now.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Tklp> Remember to keep it quiet, don't tell anyone because when we do    บ
 บ         come in, we are coming in with a BANG!                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** [RI-X] has left channel #Reflux                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Some of you might be asking yourselves, why would ROR change its      บ
 บ  name to Reflux?  After all, ROR has been around for about 10 months now,  บ
 บ  and that does give it a reputation as being a stable group (even though   บ
 บ  that might not be the case).  Tklp has worked very hard in giving ROR a   บ
 บ  good name, he's very good at what he does.  I have to give credit where   บ
 บ  it's due, he was a pro at making the Quake Beta look like the Quake       บ
 บ  Final.  He even fooled me until Jay Wilbur from iD Software told me that  บ
 บ  ROR's release was not the final version.  Not every lamer can pull lame   บ
 บ  tricks like that, only really special lamers are stupid enough to do      บ
 บ  something like that.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When word (thanks to RCN) got around that ROR's release of Quake was  บ
 บ  an intentional fake, many of the major bulletin boards and ftp sites      บ
 บ  decided to pool together and blacklist all ROR releases.  That made Tklp  บ
 บ  shit a brick, a real big brick, or rather, a small house.  Nobody would   บ
 บ  let him upload his fake releases anymore, because ROR*.* was blacklisted  บ
 บ  on so many popular boards.  Tklp then decided that it was time to change  บ
 บ  his group name from ROR to RLX.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Siteops and sysops, if you were smart enough to ban ROR*.*, well,     บ
 บ  you might as well change ban RLX*.* too.  There's really no difference    บ
 บ  between ROR and RLX except for the name.  I'll even show you the old ROR  บ
 บ  nfo and the new RLX nfo, and you can tell that RLX is still led by Tklp,  บ
 บ  and that many of the same ROR members are also RLX members.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ              to check on it yet.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <CrzyHorse> I didn't think it was in the channel though.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Then that must have been something else.  What happened with  บ
 บ              you then?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <CrzyHorse> There is a board in my area code that the sysops here and     บ
 บ              the sysops there are friends.  A long time ago, we said that  บ
 บ              we would not take each others affiliations.  We made an       บ
 บ              agreement and also would not be in the same groups.  We felt  บ
 บ              it was better for the area code to have a lot of              บ
 บ              affiliations rather than just 2 or 3.  So, the sysops of      บ
 บ              that board learned how to supply games and are doing so for   บ
 บ              Razor 1911.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Ah.. so this is a competition for suppliers between Prestige  บ
 บ              and Razor 1911?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <CrzyHorse> Prestige made it seem like they were going to offer the       บ
 บ              sysops of that board membership in Prestige as member         บ
 บ              boards, but because of the agreement that we made, the        บ
 บ              sysops would have been unable to accept the Prestige offer.   บ
 บ              They would not have accepted anyway, even if Prestige asked,  บ
 บ              they have ALWAYS wanted to be in Razor 1911 and would not     บ
 บ              leave.  But because of the agreement, Prestige didn't want    บ
 บ              to be tied up so they said that they didn't want our board    บ
 บ              anymore.  Then, they rethought it and offered our board as a  บ
 บ              member board but not as a Courier HQ anymore.  We declined.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> I see.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <CrzyHorse> So that is the story.  And I think it is total political      บ
 บ              group bullshit.  They didn't even ask the sysops of the       บ
 บ              board.  They were thinking.  If the original agreement        บ
 บ              between the sysops was not there, we could have gotten the    บ
 บ              Razor 1911 suppliers in Prestige.  But the truth is, if the   บ
 บ              Razor 1911 sysops REALLY wanted in the Prestige, they would   บ
 บ              have come to Prestige and said, "Look, we want in Prestige,"  บ
 บ              and then we would have worked something out.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Who's the sysop of this Razor 1911 board?                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <CrzyHorse> You figure it out.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Ah, come on, don't be a bad sport.  How am I supposed to      บ
 บ              know who's who?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <CrzyHorse> Look in the Razor 1911 nfo.  You'll figure it out I am sure.  บ
 บ              I can't tell you everything, no fun in that.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I never did find the time to investigate on that matter, but the      บ
 บ  names aren't really important.  This log file shows that games group      บ
 บ  politics all revolve around one thing, if you can supply games, you're    บ
 บ  important.  If you can't, then you're just another Crazy Horse, you       บ
 บ  might run a 10 node board, you might have helped the group in the past    บ
 บ  by being their Courier HQ, and you might even be as loyal to the group    บ
 บ  as a son is to a father, but in the end, none of that matters.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm just glad I don't have to worry about supplying the latest        บ
 บ  releases out for a games group.  And if you're a supplier, find a group   บ
 บ  that likes you for YOU, and not because you can supply, you'll be         บ
 บ  happier that way.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ

      ฿                   ฿            a r t i c l e s !
                    ฐ฿                 ฐ฿
                     ฿                   ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Temp Directories                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      About a year and a half ago, the Internet swept over the warez scene  บ
 บ  and introduced to it a new form of transporting files.  It boasted a new  บ
 บ  speed at which software could be distributed.  Everybody would log onto   บ
 บ  a UNIX shell account and transfer files at speeds exceeding 100k/s.       บ
 บ  Then the WWW came about and people all switched over to SLIP/PPP          บ
 บ  accounts.  And where did these "super fast speeds" all go?  Straight      บ
 บ  down the drain.  Now 85% of the users on the Internet are logged on to    บ
 บ  accounts that can push no more than 3k/s, and their end users are still   บ
 บ  boasting speeds of 100k/s, and I sit here confused.  These accounts are   บ
 บ  as gay as AOL accounts, slow!                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      But there are still a select few of us that do use the traditional    บ
 บ  UNIX shell account.  Admittedly, it's a little harder to use than the     บ
 บ  PPP account, and it takes a few tries to get to know, but once one gets   บ
 บ  a shell account to work well and knows how to use it to perfection, the   บ
 บ  Internet is just a toy to be played with.  One of the great toys is the   บ
 บ  infamous temp directory.  A temp directory is a location on a UNIX shell  บ
 บ  provider on which big files can be stored for temporary use.  All         บ
 บ  providers have the directory, but it becomes useful beyond practicality   บ
 บ  on the really big ones.  Most UNIX shell accounts include a 5 MB disk     บ
 บ  quota.  This generally means that the average meggage of the files        บ
 บ  stored in the directory at a certain calculation time for the month       บ
 บ  cannot exceed 5 megabytes.  Some more stingy providers restrict shell     บ
 บ  accounts to 5 megabytes of quota at any given time, meaning that any      บ
 บ  file transfer exceeding 5 megabytes in size will be cancelled upon        บ
 บ  reaching this size limit.  These accounts are what I would refer to as    บ
 บ  "piles of crap" accounts.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We all know, however, that sometimes a HUGE release (size-wise) is    บ
 บ  released and we want to download it overnight, but don't want it to get   บ
 บ  added onto our quota size average.  In this case, the temp drive may be   บ
 บ  put to use.  On most providers, this directory is /temp but that is       บ
 บ  often a link to a directory such as /hack2/tmp.  Either one works.  Any   บ
 บ  user desiring a place to store some files for a temporary amount of time  บ
 บ  can resort to using this directory.  Many providers allocate a hard       บ
 บ  drive just for this directory, which is why it can also be referred to    บ
 บ  as a temp drive.  The user can copy his/her files to this directory and   บ
 บ  proceed to download them, quota-free.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Still, some of us just want MORE from our temp drives!  The big       บ
 บ  providers, the ones with members from around the country, the ones with   บ
 บ  many warez-affiliated members, are the ones that can give us that extra   บ
 บ  knack.  Some of the big providers don't care about warez on their         บ
 บ  drives, or are just not aware of their existence.  Some just choose not   บ
 บ  to interfere in the activity of their users, as that would imply          บ
 บ  censorship.  These providers tend to have temp drives filled to the top   บ
 บ  with the latest warez.  Of course, if you're quiet, you might even be     บ
 บ  able to snaggle some of these warez for yourself!  You can copy them to   บ
 บ  your home directory (cd ~) for download, you can copy them to another     บ
 บ  temp drive directory that only you have user rights to (man chmod for     บ
 บ  help on how to accomplish this), or, as courtesy would have it, you       บ
 บ  could just leech the warez directly from the directory in which they      บ
 บ  exist.  This is often the best thing to do as far as netiquette goes,     บ
 บ  because you won't be filling up the provider's drive with duplicate       บ
 บ  files.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyway, a cheery hello to all of you out there that still use shell   บ
 บ  accounts, we know they're the best (hehe), and check out your temp        บ
 บ  drive, if you're lucky, you'll find more than you expected!               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

     ฿ ฿  ฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿    ฿  r c n          ฿฿ ฿฿
   ฿ ฐ  ฿               ฿   ฿ฐ   ฿
 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿       ฿        
                             ฐ฿฿฿฿฿    ฿ฐ฿฿฿฿
 ฿ฐ      ฿ฐ      ฿฿฿ฐ                                 ฿฿฿
      ฿                   ฿            a r t i c l e s !
                    ฐ฿                 ฐ฿
                     ฿                   ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Xenon's Life in RCN                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The past month has been filled with a multitude of emails inquiring   บ
 บ  about Xenon, the RCN coder.  The extremists expressed religious           บ
 บ  attachments to Xenon, "Xenon is my God!!!"  Others expressed more subtle  บ
 บ  desires, "Xenon is one of the best coders I've seen in the scene!"  Some  บ
 บ  expressed a concern for the real-life Xenon, "So what's he like in real   บ
 บ  life?!"  And others just wanted something in return, "Can you like send   บ
 บ  me the RCN source code?  Uhuh uhuh uhuhuhuh.."  So I present to you, the  บ
 บ  life of a coder.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Xenon is 16 years old, yet his programming skills greatly exceed      บ
 บ  those of many third year college students.  His first programming         บ
 บ  experience was on an old Timex Sinclair 1000 computer at the age of just  บ
 บ  5 years.  When I found this out, my face was of pure astonishment.  When  บ
 บ  I was busy blowing soap bubbles into the wind, he was writing a program   บ
 บ  to blow up the world.  Xenon explained, however, that at 5, he never      บ
 บ  really made his own programs, but rather "modified the work of others."   บ
 บ  He said this quite nonchalantly and apparently didn't think anything of   บ
 บ  it.  Xenon then moved on to the Commodore 64 when he was 7, and by now,   บ
 บ  became quite an experienced coder.  He once even coded a game much like   บ
 บ  Pacman, from scratch.  He explained to me that he was a proud 7 year old  บ
 บ  when he found out how to use sprites for smoother scrolling and better    บ
 บ  looking graphics.  I was perplexed.  At 9, Xenon acquired a super dooper  บ
 บ  Apple IIe.  WOW.  His BASIC skills were now running at a MILLION hertz,   บ
 บ  but with a new and improved interface... or not.  He was still cookin'    บ
 บ  at a million hertz, but as unlike the Commodore 64, the graphics were     บ
 บ  easier to implement.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In 6th grade, at 11 years of age, Xenon discovered the awesome        บ
 บ  capabilities of the IBM/PC XT.  This baby was pushing da bitz at 4.77     บ
 บ  Megahertz.  So much for color graphics, but 720x348 was a resolution      บ
 บ  previously unheard of.  He darted to school to let the rest of his        บ
 บ  classmates know about his new discovery, but for some reason, they        บ
 บ  seemed disinterested.  They were more concerned in the upcoming Sex-ed    บ
 บ  class.  The bell rang, and it was time to go home... or better yet, to    บ
 บ  jet down to the garage to see if he could scrounge up some of his dad's   บ
 บ  old "Compute!" magazines.  Then, back to his room so he could type in     บ
 บ  some of the included programs and see what they did.  If I haven't made   บ
 บ  it obvious enough, Xenon was a happy child.  Xenon's brother, who, by     บ
 บ  now was about to graduate from high school, had acquired a version of     บ
 บ  this totally k-rad new programming language called Turbo Pascal.  He      บ
 บ  wasn't so thrilled about learning a new language, but then he noticed     บ
 บ  one of his brother's programs, and found out about a new word to add to   บ
 บ  his now 11 year old vocabulary, COMPILE!  Long as it may have seemed, it  บ
 บ  would turn out to be a key word in his life.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Turbo Pascal was faster, and could really take advantage of his 4.77  บ
 บ  Mhz XT.  It was now easier to perform more complex tasks (well, as        บ
 บ  complex as an 11 year old mind can do).  This was cool.  A new thing to   บ
 บ  do in his spare time.  He could draw lines, make boxes, fill them in,     บ
 บ  make patterns, and even use fonts!  He was now in 8th grade, and again    บ
 บ  he went to class to report of his new findings.  But once more, his       บ
 บ  classmates were not interested.  When they were thinking about boobs, he  บ
 บ  was thinking about booleans.  When they were talking about girls, he was  บ
 บ  talking aboug GotoXY's.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      More recently, namely in his Junior year, Xenon met Rebel Chicken,    บ
 บ  and Hitex and Rebel Chicken found a more useful way of using Xenon's      บ
 บ  talents.  Instead of having him code random programs "just for fun,"  we  บ
 บ  used it for extensive work with graphics and sound.  So now, you are      บ
 บ  running a program taking advantage of all of his skills.  Let me          บ
 บ  continue by explaining a few things about the coding in RCN.  I am doing  บ
 บ  this in response to the many letters to the editors that I have received  บ
 บ  in this past week.  Many of you have requested to know how RCN is coded.  บ
 บ  What the backbone of it is, and, most importantly, to see its source      บ
 บ  code.  I will try to answer all of your questions here, except, of        บ
 บ  course, the last one <grin>.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN is coded in Turbo Pascal v7.0 for DOS.  Many rumors have erupted  บ
 บ  that we code it completely in Assembly (ASM).  Those are completely       บ
 บ  untrue, and there's a very good reason for why they are.  It would be     บ
 บ  stupid to.  Coding in 100% ASM takes an extremely long amount of time     บ
 บ  and there are no known benefits to doing so for something such as RCN.    บ
 บ  Turbo Pascal v7.0 does a wonderful job of implementing inline assembly    บ
 บ  (ASM code within the Pascal code), and there is no reason to dispute      บ
 บ  that.  The bulk of the interface is coded in Pascal, with the single      บ
 บ  exception of the text scroller.  That involves changing the vertical      บ
 บ  offset of the text screen, a process called "panning."  Nifty, eh?  We    บ
 บ  use the BIN format for storing the text screens, simply because it is     บ
 บ  easier to implement into the code, and is one less thing to worry about.  บ
 บ  Well, sort of.  It then poses the problem of dealing with files           บ
 บ  exceeding 64k (in the extracted EXE, BIN files compress extremely well).  บ
 บ  Memory is accessed in 64k blocks, and Xenon has implemented impressive    บ
 บ  swapping algorithms that barely cause any delay when viewing the          บ
 บ  magazine.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The 3D design at the beginning of RCN is probably one of the more     บ
 บ  complicated parts of Reality Check Network.  It may look simple, but it   บ
 บ  involves the manipulation of polygons on 3 axis, all the while updating   บ
 บ  light shadowing from different angles.  The color palette is constantly   บ
 บ  updating to accommodate a wide array of colors while displaying           บ
 บ  different shades of each in the spinning of a mere 3 letters.  Groovy,    บ
 บ  isn't it?  The RCN ending is the displaying of a 320x200 (we tried        บ
 บ  640x480 last week, but it made the EXE too big) graphic while doing real  บ
 บ  time rendering of a graphic effect superimposed on it.  But by far the    บ
 บ  most complex part of the ending is what to call it.  I insist it's a      บ
 บ  magnifying glass, but Rebel Chicken argues that if it were a magnifying   บ
 บ  glass, it would have a stick to hold it by.  A friend once suggested      บ
 บ  that it is an elipse of which only one side is displayed but that didn't  บ
 บ  go over too well with Xenon, so we here at RCN studios just refer to it   บ
 บ  as "the thing."                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The most impressive part of RCN is, of course, the game.  Many        บ
 บ  suggest that we have stolen Tyrian, but I beg to differ.  It never took   บ
 บ  you 30 minutes to beat one level of Tyrian.  The game engine is coded     บ
 บ  purely in ASM, merely because Xenon has yet to learn how to code a good   บ
 บ  game in Pascal and how to optimize his code so it doesn't require a       บ
 บ  Pentium Pro to run on.  The hard part is the randomizing of enemies       บ
 บ  while calculating the position of your ship and its relation to other     บ
 บ  ships and their bullets.  Without the use of ASM, all this crawled on a   บ
 บ  Pentium 100.  With all this to worry about, we decided Epic Megagames     บ
 บ  wouldn't be too discouraged if we merely "borrowed" their graphics for a  บ
 บ  few weeks.  And anyway, it's free advertising.  Moreover, the game takes  บ
 บ  a mere 30k zipped, where Tyrian takes 3 disks zipped.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN is, still, probably most amazing in its behind-the-scenes work.   บ
 บ  In RCN's Issue #12, we had 8 articles and 8 interviews, but that was      บ
 บ  about where the content ended.  All the content, of course, edited and    บ
 บ  looked over by Hitex or Rebel Chicken to insure quality in context as     บ
 บ  well as in content.  However, in RCN #14, we added reviews and charts to  บ
 บ  our to-do list, and that lead to an extreme work overload.  We decided    บ
 บ  to put Xenon to work (we don't like to see him sitting around, it makes   บ
 บ  us feel guilty).  Now, we just do all our work in a regular DOS Edit      บ
 บ  window and never worry about formatting it into a nice looking layout.    บ
 บ  We leave that up to Xenon's "RCN Helper."  Hah, and you thought we        บ
 บ  actually slaved over an Acid Draw screen for hours on end.  Hell no, DOS  บ
 บ  Edit is much better <grin>.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It seems that technology has always just barely kept up with the      บ
 บ  need of today's software, and the same can be said about RCN.  Our        บ
 บ  coding has always just barely kept up with our needs.  Using the old      บ
 บ  system of publication, RCN would never make it out the door in one week.  บ
 บ  Using Xenon's latest coding, however, we have the resources needed to     บ
 บ  keep up with the influx of submitted articles and interviews.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Xenon is definitely one of the scene's greatest, we all know that     บ
 บ  without his great coding, RCN would just be an oversized version of       บ
 บ  Inquisition (available on WWW.RCN.ORG), and none of us would want that!   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

    ฿฿        ฐ       ฿฿฿ฐ                      ฐ฿฿฿
     ฿ ฿  ฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿    ฿  r c n          ฿฿ ฿฿
   ฿ ฐ  ฿               ฿   ฿ฐ   ฿
 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿       ฿        
                             ฐ฿฿฿฿฿    ฿ฐ฿฿฿฿
 ฿ฐ      ฿ฐ      ฿฿฿ฐ                                 ฿฿฿
      ฿                   ฿            a r t i c l e s !
                    ฐ฿                 ฐ฿
                     ฿                   ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Wart                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : A Warez School?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The most common way people get started in the warez scene is not for  บ
 บ  prestige or privilge.  It is for a couple of applications or games that   บ
 บ  they're after and wish to grab without having to pay for them.  When      บ
 บ  they first go into warez rooms on IRC and start trading they suddenly     บ
 บ  feel an immense surge of power from a forbidden well.  When they see      บ
 บ  what's on offer, regardless of how big, whether they actually need it or  บ
 บ  not, indeed if they will ever use it after downloading it.  They just     บ
 บ  download it anyway, just another bargaining chip to bring to the channel  บ
 บ  for the games or utils they want.  It's become the rudimentry currency    บ
 บ  of the internet underground.  The months most publicised releases always  บ
 บ  being the most sought after.  Then after this introductory phase when     บ
 บ  they have all the software they want they still frequent the channels     บ
 บ  semi-serving to the new traders, a cry of, "What do you want?" will       บ
 บ  always respond with, "What have you got?" when they are at this phase.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once they tire of this level of interaction on the warez scene they   บ
 บ  move onto trying to provide services for others.  Serv-u ftp sites over   บ
 บ  28.8 are a common sight as well as mIRC fserves.  What with all the       บ
 บ  obvious channel names taken they create a new one and invite people onto  บ
 บ  it in the hope it will gain popularity and will become a permanent        บ
 บ  fixture on the IRC landscape.  However with their inexperience in         บ
 บ  scrpiting and creating a bot these channels tend to blossom and fold      บ
 บ  with the founder's appearences on the network.  More determined           บ
 บ  providers find suppliers outside of IRC and setup small warez groups      บ
 บ  releasing or couriering.  These groups don't last very long but with      บ
 บ  perserverence they will get offered a place in a medium sized group and   บ
 บ  start in the scene proper.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After a while playing in these leagues watching all the bigger,       บ
 บ  better groups beat you to releasing and couriering because all the        บ
 บ  members who have something to offer are already working for these         บ
 บ  groups.  If you're lucky you'll catch a break and pull of something       บ
 บ  special which will grab the attention of some of the bigger groups then   บ
 บ  you'll get pulled into the big leagues and swap in and out of groups for  บ
 บ  a while until settling in to a group where some of the people they knew   บ
 บ  before in the little leagues have settled as well then it pretty much     บ
 บ  ends there until they quit the scene.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The above bears resemblence to the average life of a warez trader.    บ
 บ  There are some variations, such as moving into the realms of emags based  บ
 บ  on the scene.  A sort of niche in the market, if you will.  This fine     บ
 บ  magazine bears proof to it.  In my opinion, a lot of time could be saved  บ
 บ  if the scene was better organised at the basic level.  Letting these      บ
 บ  warez pups (not my choice of term, BTW) run riot in the channels without  บ
 บ  any guidance means they will mature into the scene with anarchistic       บ
 บ  tendancies which lead to immature behavior such as channel takeovers,     บ
 บ  and other things such as narking and all kinds of things which            บ
 บ  ultimately sully the scene.  I realize that the very nature of the        บ
 บ  Internet is that of anarchy, however with a little self-restraint we      บ
 บ  might end up with better traders, couriers, and suppliers whose           บ
 บ  decisions are made with sober judgement and experience, not with          บ
 บ  immature emotion and threating behavior.  I know it may never happen,     บ
 บ  however I'd like to propose an idea to the scene as whole with I believe  บ
 บ  would lead to an enrichment of the scene while still retaining that       บ
 บ  wild, forbbiden side that entices many to it.  Heres what I suggest...    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I realize that many of the scene leaders may have grievences against  บ
 บ  each other, and that this may be a reason why this idea would never be    บ
 บ  taken up as it requires an agreement between a large number of groups of  บ
 บ  a standard.  The thing is you'd never know what someone was capable of    บ
 บ  until you've given them the chance to prove themselves.  The elitist      บ
 บ  nature of the majority of scene members counteract this.  Their pride     บ
 บ  won't allow them to accept that there is anyone better than them.  I      บ
 บ  suggest that an independent body be created to handle the training of     บ
 บ  these warez pups (again, not my choice of term) and their progress and    บ
 บ  abilities monitored, and at the end of their training some sort of award  บ
 บ  or recognition that they are in some way qualified to do a particular     บ
 บ  job in a warez group.  Of course for something like this to be taken      บ
 บ  seriously a lot of groups would have to agree to liason with this         บ
 บ  independent body in order for an appraisal of the applicant or maybe      บ
 บ  indeed groups would solicit this independent body for likely candidates   บ
 บ  whenever an opening in their group became available.  If a few groups     บ
 บ  would agree to recognise the recognition this independent body bestowed   บ
 บ  on them the scene would be better organized as this training could        บ
 บ  encompass a wide range of things from FTP methods to general behavior in  บ
 บ  a warez group.  I realize of course that this is a dream that will never  บ
 บ  happen due to the already choactic nature of the scene, however if        บ
 บ  enough respected and determined people got together it could happen       บ
 บ  groups could even begin to submit required techniques to the independent  บ
 บ  body for inclusion in their training.  How are these pups ever going to   บ
 บ  make it up the ladder without some sort of start that anyone with a bit   บ
 บ  of determination and skill could get.  You could count on the fingers of  บ
 บ  one hand the number of groups that provide internal training facilities.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The only way to implement this would be to have it set up with all    บ
 บ  senior members and advisors independent of any other group to insure a    บ
 บ  degree of fair play, then the liason members of the groups that would     บ
 บ  recognise any of the qualifications handed out.  Then of course the       บ
 บ  students themselves who would see it as a road into a warez group with a  บ
 บ  solid reputation.  It would take some time for the standard to become     บ
 บ  accepted practise.  However if more people were trained up at the         บ
 บ  begginer we wouldn't see any of this lamer crap that the elitist types    บ
 บ  come out with.  Just because they've been in the scene longer and know    บ
 บ  all their stuff doesn't mean that in three months down the line, this     บ
 บ  supposed lamer wouldn't be running a kick ass warez group and the         บ
 บ  original so-called elite come knocking on his door.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Everybody came from the bottom rung, only those lucky enough to       บ
 บ  catch a break and get or become a good suppiler let their heads swell     บ
 บ  and prat around being k-rad elite.  Never forget where you came from,     บ
 บ  you were there once, they are there now, go on.  Give them a helping      บ
 บ  hand, you won't regret it.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Undinism                                                      บ
 บ    Subject : The Stars Tell All!                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, here comes a letter from one of its members, not very active    บ
 บ  lately due to personal shit going on. I was very surprised how two of     บ
 บ  your star signs applied directly in an abstract warez <> real life way    บ
 บ  to me and my present situation.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am an Aries and the part regarding now comes a close to the         บ
 บ  sexiest part of my life seems to sum up how I feel at the moment.  My     บ
 บ  ex-girlfriend is a Taurus and she broke up with me on last Tuesday.  So   บ
 บ  that's the issue being more easily resolved shit over.  I guess the star  บ
 บ  signs were one week late but the days were right.  I am writing as I      บ
 บ  feel the warez/pc life had a major part in the breaking up.  It all       บ
 บ  dated back to some months when I decided to courier my ass off for NBC.   บ
 บ  I was dcc'ing 15+ gig PER day with 3-5 dcc's kicking non-stop.  After     บ
 บ  that I spent nearly 50-70% of my time on the PC (as most people will      บ
 บ  know).  I did have a VERY good looking girlfriend who did love me and     บ
 บ  all that shit.  But it all came to a head as she missed spending time     บ
 บ  with me and decided to wait and see if i would stop.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, of course without her telling me to spend more time with her    บ
 บ  besides sex (guess us males cant read minds like we're supposed to), I    บ
 บ  stayed on the PC and couriered more and more.  IRC was also taking a lot  บ
 บ  of time.  Anyway to get to the point, yes its fun to courier, chat, and   บ
 บ  dcc on the net but don't let it interfere with your real/love life.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, I am now single again and don't feel like spending too much     บ
 บ  time on IRC or FTP sites.  I guess moderation is the key and realise      บ
 บ  this even though you're saving $$$$$ by download warez, are you actually  บ
 บ  saving $$ as would you have brought that lame game or util that took 5    บ
 บ  hours to download because of size and shit.  Anway here's to the warez    บ
 บ  scene and I hope it thrives (as more males in the scene = more females    บ
 บ  not getting sex).  Thats my 2 cents for once.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* A LONG serving RCN member and not even senior, hehe...               บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Tuxedo Mask                                                   บ
 บ    Subject : Computer and Television Monitors, Roled into One?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most of the parts in my main desktop PC get replaced every year or    บ
 บ  two by something newer and cooler, but I've been staring at the same 17"  บ
 บ  Nanao video monitor since I started chatting on IRC back in 1993.  Only   บ
 บ  the case, the keyboard and the floppy drives have survived longer.  Good  บ
 บ  monitors aren't cheap, but if recent history is any guide, that might be  บ
 บ  the one part of your computer that you can think of as a long term        บ
 บ  investment.  VGA and SVGA monitors have used the same cables and          บ
 บ  connectors for a decade now, and a top notch monitor from the early       บ
 บ  90's, with a .28mm dot pitch and a 64kHz maximum horizontal scan rate,    บ
 บ  still looks great by today's standards.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      About those numbers, we all know that computer images are composed    บ
 บ  of small blocks known as "pixels," but the screen of a color monitor is   บ
 บ  also a composite.  It's made up of many small red, green, and blue        บ
 บ  phospor dots, and the distance from dot to dot is known as the "dot       บ
 บ  pitch," usually measured in millimeters.  Hey, when I first got my PC, I  บ
 บ  didn't know what these meant.  So I was just about as lost as any lamer   บ
 บ  who found himself stuck in a #WarezX channel not knowing what "xdcc       บ
 บ  list" meant.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most PCs are set up to display about 80 to 90 pixels per inch.  If    บ
 บ  you're handy with the metric system, you'll see that each pixel covers a  บ
 บ  bit more than a quarter of a milimeter, which is equal to a dot pitch of  บ
 บ  .25mm.  That dot pitch is found on some monitors, but .28mm is            บ
 บ  considered acceptable.  The smaller and more closely spaced the dots      บ
 บ  are, the sharper the picture will be, and the more the monitor will       บ
 บ  cost.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Like movies and television, computer video is drawn a sequence of     บ
 บ  frames, one after another.  The number of frames drawn each second is     บ
 บ  the vertical scan rate.  The horizontal scan rate counts rows of pixels   บ
 บ  or "scan lines," per second.  These scan rates are controlled by the      บ
 บ  computer's video card, but the monitor still has to be able to keep up    บ
 บ  with the signal it receives.  A monitor's scan rates are listed as upper  บ
 บ  and lower limits.  If it's fed video outside of this range, the monitor   บ
 บ  won't be able to stay in sync, and the picture will appear to rool on     บ
 บ  the screen.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The vertical scanning rate is rarely a problem.  Video cards usually  บ
 บ  operate between 60 and 75Hz, well within the range of most monitors.      บ
 บ  But that frame rate also affects the horizontal scan rate, which you can  บ
 บ  compute by multiplying the number of frames per second by the virtual     บ
 บ  resolution, adding in about 30 invisible lines scanned between video      บ
 บ  frames.  If a program runs at 1,204x768 resolution, the video card is     บ
 บ  feeding the monitor 768 lines of video per frame.  At a frame rate of     บ
 บ  72Hz, that means the monitor has to scan more than 57,000 lines per       บ
 บ  second, or 57kHz.  High resolution monitors usually have maximum          บ
 บ  horizontal rates of 64kHz or more.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A few features are found on newer monitors which didn't exist at the  บ
 บ  beginning of the decade.  Most support VESA's Display Data Channel        บ
 บ  (DDC), which lets the PC tell the monitor to enter a low power, energy    บ
 บ  saving sleep mode.  The latest designs are also Plug-n-PLay compatible,   บ
 บ  allowing the operating system to detect the type of monitor that's        บ
 บ  connected.  The biggest change we've seen in monitors has been in         บ
 บ  prices, particularly in the larger sized tubes.  A big monitor's extra    บ
 บ  display area really helps when you're displaying 800x600 pixels or more   บ
 บ  on the screen.  Microsoft Windows has made it easier to use a video       บ
 บ  card's high resolution display modes, making larger monitors much more    บ
 บ  popular.  Economy of scale has pushed prices down to the point where 17"  บ
 บ  monitors now start in the low $600's.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      That's not bad, but it isn't exactly cheap either, especially when    บ
 บ  you can get a name brand 25" television set for less than $250.  But      บ
 บ  there are a couple of reasons why televisions cost so much less, so many  บ
 บ  of them are built, and so little is expected of them.  No matter how big  บ
 บ  a TV screen is, it only has to display a standard 525 line, 60 frames     บ
 บ  per second video signal.  PC monitor designers assume that you'll want    บ
 บ  90 or so pixels per inch resolution on any monitor, so a bigger screen    บ
 บ  means more pixels.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The typical 21" monitor has to support resolutions as high as         บ
 บ  1,600x1,280 pixels, which boosts the horizontal scanning frequency up to  บ
 บ  around 90kHz.  The markets that need a monitor like that, CAD,            บ
 บ  publishing, and professional graphics, are very small compared to the PC  บ
 บ  market in general, it isn't so surprising that 21" monitors sell for      บ
 บ  close to $2,000.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      But there are some signs that we might be seeing large monitors in    บ
 บ  the future that aren't targeted toward such narrow markets.  Toshiba      บ
 บ  offers a 20" television that also functions as a SVGA monitor for around  บ
 บ  $700.  Its maximum resolution of 640x480 pixels isn't much of a problem   บ
 บ  for game playing, but it could be limiting for general use.  Also,        บ
 บ  Gateway 2000 has announced it plans to offer a VCR-sized system called    บ
 บ  Destination, complete with a 31" monitor and a built-in TV tuner.         บ
 บ  Expect to pay about $4,000 late this fall.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And then there's High Definition Telivision.  The Digital HDTV Grand  บ
 บ  Alliance proposal, recommended by the FCC's Advisory Committee on         บ
 บ  Advanced Television Service last November, still awaits final approval    บ
 บ  by the FCC.  But the system's highest resolution is 1920x1080, with a     บ
 บ  cinematic 16:9 width to height ratio instead of the now standard 4:3.     บ
 บ  If HDTV catches on, we'll all have television sets that put most current  บ
 บ  PC video monitors to shame.  By the most optimistic estimates, HDTV       บ
 บ  should really take off sometime early in the next century.  Maybe then    บ
 บ  I'll be able to put this old monitor out to pasture.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

      ฐ                      ฿฿ฐ            ฿฿฿
  ฿  ฿฿  r c n ฿   ฐ  ฿฿฿      ฿฿          ฿ ฿
  ฿   ฿฿       ฿  ฿    ฿   ฿ฐ      ฐ  ฿
 ฐฐฐ ฿   ฿ฐ ฐ ฿ ฐฐฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐฐฐ  ฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐ ฐฐ
  ฐ฿  ฿฿฿฿฿฿  ฿      ฿       ฿ ฿       
   ฿     ฿       ฿         ฿฿฿฿฿   ฿฿    ฿ฐ฿ฐ฿฿฿฿
            ฿฿฿฿฿     ฿฿       ฿฿฿ฐ                        ฿ฐ฿฿

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/06/96 -> 06/12/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/13/96 -> 06/19/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 06/26/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
