 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/13/96 -> 06/19/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 06/26/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/26/96 -> 07/03/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RoadRebel,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      About the disk size/number of disks limit, here are my feelings.  It  บ
 บ  is getting to where the 40 disk limit is hard to match.  Game sizes keep  บ
 บ  growing, as do utils sizes, we can't keep the limit so low.  It would be  บ
 บ  like saying my foot is growing, but I can only buy size 10 shoes.  There  บ
 บ  are many utils coming out now that are very large, especially some of     บ
 บ  the operating systems, you don't want only part of an operating system,   บ
 บ  you want the whole thing.  I think the size of disks should stay small    บ
 บ  enough to fit on 1 normal 1.44 meg floppy.  There should be a group of    บ
 บ  one or 2 leaders from each games and utils group, that have a monthly     บ
 บ  meeting on IRC, for each of their type of releases.  They could discuss   บ
 บ  things like this, I personally think the current limit for games should   บ
 บ  be 50, and utils 60.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Manic                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Manic,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      50 disks for a game is fine, if the game is worth it, but when they   บ
 บ  go higher it better be a GOOD game.  But I think that this 1.4 meg stuff  บ
 บ  is shit.  There is really no point to it anymore, no one uses disks.      บ
 บ  BUT, we need to come up with a new standard for relasing that all groups  บ
 บ  can agree with.  I personally think thaty switching to 3 meg disks would  บ
 บ  be the best, BUT it won't happen anytime soon of course.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm sure you have probably read about this topic in a computer game   บ
 บ  magazine, but I'm telling you straight out, from warez kid, to warez      บ
 บ  kid.  Many Groups like to release the games that are big, and are over    บ
 บ  at least 30 megs.  That is how it seems to be to me.  I myself solely     บ
 บ  judge a game on how long I play it, which sooner or later leads to        บ
 บ  "gameplay."  If companies such as Origin keep releasing such big games,   บ
 บ  like Wing Commander 4 (6 cd's), who is going to want to rip that, and     บ
 บ  release that?  Exactly, no one.  My point is, I understand it is not the  บ
 บ  releasing groups faults releasing big games, like Vikings, and Front      บ
 บ  Page Sports Baseball 96 by Razor 1911.  I like to courier warez, for DSC  บ
 บ  (Dark Side Couriers) and for PTA (Power Trading Arsenal) but aside from   บ
 บ  all the couriering, I also like to play the games.  I don't think I am    บ
 บ  the only one either.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As a tip for releasing groups, look for games that you can play,      บ
 บ  instead of watching, because most of the big games are packed with        บ
 บ  boring, full motion video.  Don't get me wrong, full motion video was     บ
 บ  awesome, when it first came out.  But now that FMV is overplayed, and is  บ
 บ  found in most games, it is more boring than exciting.  Also, I have seen  บ
 บ  a couple games where FMV has been perfectly filled in, to occupy ONE cd,  บ
 บ  and an occasional TWO cds, but when you get to 4,5, and 6 cds, what the   บ
 บ  hell?  To be totally honest with you, I had more fun playing the game     บ
 บ  packed in the RCN E-Mags, than I did playing Wing Commander III.  If      บ
 บ  more games were released that you could play, more people would play      บ
 บ  them.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Retix                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Retix,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I agree somewhat, BUT, I have played some larger games that I think   บ
 บ  were ripped perfect.  A good case is Afterlife by Lucas Arts, the game    บ
 บ  was 40 disks which made most people avoid it, BUT, I leeched it and it    บ
 บ  was WELL worth the time, the only thing really ripped was the scenarios.  บ
 บ  I asked Prestige to release them seperate, but of course I have leeched   บ
 บ  huge shit that sucked.  As for FMV, most of it BLOWS!  Rip that shit      บ
 บ  outa there!                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RoadRebel,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In concern to the file size of many programs, I feel that it is a     บ
 บ  waste to release programs more than like 20 disks because on my BBS I     บ
 บ  noticed if I put a file online that is bigger than 12 disks, it rarely    บ
 บ  gets downloaded unless the hype is so good for instance like Duke Nukem.  บ
 บ  Why would someone waste their time downloading something for maybe 3 to   บ
 บ  4 days and then have it needing a fix or not working all together.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most people that I deal with on my system don't even have the         บ
 บ  greatest computers with hard drives of like 800 megs.  Why are they       บ
 บ  going to want something taking up like 200 megs???  I think it is good    บ
 บ  to make some CD-rips but do them in parts like some groups are beginning  บ
 บ  to do like make it a mininum CD-rip then for all those who have the time  บ
 บ  and space make a sound addon then a graphics addon so that everyone who   บ
 บ  wants to enjoy the game can have a chance to.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For instance, people on my BBS want a Need for Speed SE minimum       บ
 บ  CD-Rip because 56 disks is just way too many to download.  I think        บ
 บ  bigger releases are good though for Internet traders with shells because  บ
 บ  they have the ability to grab the files a lot quicker.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  HBKid                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear HBKid,                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, I will leech anything off a bbs if I have the time, BUT, when   บ
 บ  I was a sysop, I know that some people wouldn't go over like 10 disks so  บ
 บ  I know what you are saying.  I also think Need for Speed SE was a waste   บ
 บ  of time, I mean come on.  I think we would feel better about these huge   บ
 บ  games if the release groups would use their minds and look at what they   บ
 บ  are releasing first.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ

 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน

 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There has been a lot of crap said about IRC operators in RCN lately,  บ
 บ  and a lot more said about them in channel #RCN.  I'd like to begin by     บ
 บ  saying that IRC ops are NOT our enemies.  Sure, we've all ran into them,  บ
 บ  and we've all sworn revenge at one point or another, but if you know how  บ
 บ  to deal with them, it isn't that big of a deal.  Let me offer a few       บ
 บ  suggestions.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      IRC ops do NOT take out personal vendettas.  When they /kill you,     บ
 บ  they are doing their job.  Only once was I mistakenly /killed and not     บ
 บ  apologized too.  They have a rather difficult job to do.  You've got to   บ
 บ  remember that not everyone uses mass cloning to flood people and stuff.   บ
 บ  People don't know anything about it, and those people shouldn't have to   บ
 บ  put up with it.  IRC ops are trying to keep IRC up and running for        บ
 บ  beginners.  Back in the day EfNet was created, it was just that.          บ
 บ  However with the adding of more servers and the attraction IRC had too    บ
 บ  good coders/hackers, people found ways to take advantages of bugs in      บ
 บ  servers.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      DO NOT RUN CLONES.  It's that freaking simple.  If you are so lame    บ
 บ  you can't take out a channel with a time stamp collider, foreign          บ
 บ  servers, or some ICMP flooding, then don't bother coming in to harass     บ
 บ  people with your clones.  There are so many people who think crap like    บ
 บ  textbox and smoke are the coolest things around, but think about it, if   บ
 บ  they were, why would they be freely distributed?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Understand that IRC ops are just doing their job.  If they /kill      บ
 บ  you, apologize, show you don't hold it against them.  They don't sit      บ
 บ  there /kill'ing people going "hehehHEEHEHEhehehehheh yeah cool cool die   บ
 บ  die heehehaehHEHEHE."  No, they are simply trying to keep EfNet free of   บ
 บ  lamers.  Most of them don't give a crap about it, just wait until they    บ
 บ  go away and do it again.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I have made a LOT of IRC op friends.  They are pretty damn fun to     บ
 บ  talk to, if you just give them a chance.  They've helped/saved my ass on  บ
 บ  more than one occasion.  I know for a fact almost every major IRC op      บ
 บ  knows I run a crapload of bots, but they don't go around k-lining me      บ
 บ  because it isn't a big deal.  And I'm nice about it.  I've been told      บ
 บ  before by various IRC ops that another IRC op or them doesn't like my     บ
 บ  bot on their server.  So I take it off, no big deal at all.  Don't argue  บ
 บ  with individuals.  It's their machine, they can do whatever they want.    บ
 บ  One time, an oper from epix.net said I was "famous."  Heh, I did a        บ
 บ  little digging and found out I have been talked about sometimes.  The     บ
 บ  point is this, we're all bad ass IRC hackers, yeah, we know.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Try and remember, just for a second, back to your first time on IRC.  บ
 บ  Yeah, you're sitting there on your Netcom shell account, loaded ircII     บ
 บ  and wondering how the HELL you talk to people.  After spending about 2    บ
 บ  hours in the help files for ircII you figure it's time to type            บ
 บ  /channelsor whatever it was and join the first thing that caught your     บ
 บ  eye.  So you join up#!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!3yearoldsexpicswithrblchickn  บ
 บ  and expect to find some rather interesting discussion, only instead to    บ
 บ  find the channel taken over and you suddenly quit irc with "Excess        บ
 บ  Flood."  Well, you would have had NO idea how to defend yourself.  This   บ
 บ  is what IRC ops are for, to help the new guys.  Everytime an IRC op       บ
 บ  steps in to make me give back a channel I've taken over, he always says   บ
 บ  "Just let things cool down and take it back later tonight, I got a job    บ
 บ  to do here."  Or something like that.  And don't go knocking Moogle,      บ
 บ  he's killed my bots a couple times, but he saved #Sailormoon twice last   บ
 บ  week.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The point I'm trying to make here guys, is show a little              บ
 บ  understanding and cooperation.  You might make a rather powerful friend.  บ
 บ  And even if you don't, you always got someone who won't hesitate to       บ
 บ  answer a question or help you out when you are having problems.  It's     บ
 บ  what they are for, they aren't all fascist dictators, nor are they all    บ
 บ  Communists, so don't sweat it.  The last thing to remember is, NEVER      บ
 บ  flood an IRC op.  If you're that stupid, you deserve whatever you get.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Lightwing                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Lightwing,                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I don't think we said that all IRC ops are dicks, BUT, I would        บ
 บ  venture say say at least 50% are power hungry pricks that like to push    บ
 บ  people around.  But, I have also learned you can get a lot done just      บ
 บ  talking to IRC ops and not bitching at them.  As far as not ragging,      บ
 บ  Moogle goes.  I think an IRC op that make a statement "I can kill people  บ
 บ  for no reason if I want to" should be screwed with and pissed off as      บ
 บ  much as possible.  That is like a cop saying, "I can shoot people for no  บ
 บ  reason."  And you forgot to say, IRC ops all seem to know each other,     บ
 บ  and they all talk.  I am banned off servers I have never been on, and     บ
 บ  some I have never done anything wrong on!                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Road Rebel                บ

 บ      The following details your forecasts depending on your astrological   บ
 บ  sign.  Each sign designates your personal lucky numbers of the week.      บ
 บ  The following specific areas of focus include those of love and warez :   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Forecast of the week : Positive planetary movement when Jupiter is        บ
 บ  linked to Mercury will bring a new upward hill toward all goals.  Things  บ
 บ  may seem though, but your labor will prove worthwhile if you stuck with   บ
 บ  it!                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  <Aquarius> (January 21 to February 19) : Your consideration of a          บ
 บ             leadership position in a prominent warez group would benefit   บ
 บ             from a second opinion, so try to keep an open mind.  A         บ
 บ             long-term decision made later in the week will reap rewards    บ
 บ             at the end of the month.  Trust your intuition.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pisces> (February 20 to March 20) : A romantic, creative or group        บ
 บ           objective is well within your grasp as long as you have the      บ
 บ           courage and commitment to pursue it.  The Sun and Mercury in     บ
 บ           your fellow water sign of Cancer are focusing on the sunny side  บ
 บ           of life.  This is your week, enjoy it!                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Aries> (March 21 to April 20) : Friendly persuasion will serve you       บ
 บ          better than strongarm tactics this week.  Pay close attention to  บ
 บ          particulars that hang with you in group IRC channels, and avoid   บ
 บ          being excessively ambitious.  Thursday's Sun-Mercury liaison      บ
 บ          will help you resolve a conflict you may have with some friends   บ
 บ          in a group IRC channel, but you must first be willing to let      บ
 บ          others have their say.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Taurus> (April 21 to May 21) : An offer or opportunity may sound better  บ
 บ           than it really is, but it is still worth exploring.  With        บ
 บ           Mercury and Jupiter united early in the week, you may be         บ
 บ           tempted to state your terms a little too forcefully.  Listen to  บ
 บ           those who know more than you do.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Gemini> (May 22 to June 21) : With your ruler Mercury linked to both     บ
 บ           Jupiter and the Sun, you can put the finishing touches on        บ
 บ           relationships as long as you recognize the risks involved.       บ
 บ           Don't allow yourself to be sidetracked by people who have more   บ
 บ           time but less good sense than you.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Cancer> (June 22 to July 23) : Positive planetary activity in the        บ
 บ           partnership angel of your solar chart will enhance an existing   บ
 บ           relationship or pave the way for a new one.  Plans made toward   บ
 บ           the end of the week should reach fruition around the Full Moon   บ
 บ           on the 30th.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Leo> (July 24 to August 23) : You must determine whether to follow your  บ
 บ        gut feelings or take the logical approach regarding admission to a  บ
 บ        group this week.  Stick with your instincts and you won't go far    บ
 บ        wrong.  The Sun, your ruler, aligned with Mercury on Thursday will  บ
 บ        bring good advice from an unexpected direction.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Virgo> (August 24 to September 23) : Money or worries about a position   บ
 บ          in a prominent warez group may be causing you to neglect other    บ
 บ          responsibilities, but with your ruler Mercury positively linked   บ
 บ          to Jupiter and the Sun this week, you are wonderfully placed to   บ
 บ          decide how best to satisfy your personal needs.  Don't be afraid  บ
 บ          to spend time and money on yourself.  You deserve it!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Libra> (September 24 to October 23 ) : No matter how disruptive the      บ
 บ          events of the past 12 months have been, your life now appears to  บ
 บ          be on an upward curve.  In fact, this week's stimulating          บ
 บ          celestial influences should make you realize just how close you   บ
 บ          are to reaching a certain goal.  Just be careful not to overlook  บ
 บ          an important detail.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Trip                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Phreaking for the Absolute Beginner                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, you need to know that phone phreaking is ILLEGAL, and you  บ
 บ  can get in trouble for it.  But let's not worry about that yet.  For the  บ
 บ  beginner phreaker, I would suggest beige-boxing.  Beige-boxing let's you  บ
 บ  use somebody elses' phone line to make calls.  Calls that THEY have to    บ
 บ  pay for.  Here is what you are going to need :                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) A regular old touch-tone phone                                    บ
 บ      2.) A regular phone cord                                              บ
 บ      3.) Wire strippers                                                    บ
 บ      4.) 2 alligator clips                                                 บ
 บ      5.) Screwdriver                                                       บ
 บ      6.) Electrical tape                                                   บ
 บ      7.) Some 900 numbers to have fun with                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All right, so you have all this stuff and now you need to know what   บ
 บ  to do with it.  First off, you will need to cut one end of your phone     บ
 บ  cord off.  Now strip the outside covering off about 4-5 inches.  You      บ
 บ  should see a red, green, yellow and a black wire.  You will not be        บ
 บ  needing the yellow or the black one, so you can either cut them both off  บ
 บ  or leave them there.  Now you need to strip the covering off the red and  บ
 บ  the green wires.  This normally can't be done with regular                บ
 บ  wire-strippers, so I just use a knife.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After you have the RED and the GREEN wires stripped, you need to      บ
 บ  attach the green one to a green alligator clip (preferrably) and the red  บ
 บ  one to a red alligator clip.  It makes it a lot easier to match the wire  บ
 บ  colors to the color of the alligator clips (the color thing isn't         บ
 บ  important now, but it will be after you become more advanced.  Now you    บ
 บ  need to cover up this connection between the alligator clips and the      บ
 บ  wires by wrapping it with electrical tape.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, you are ready to find a house or a phone box to phreak.  It is   บ
 บ  a LOT easier and safer beige-boxing off somebody elses' house that is to  บ
 บ  beige-box a bell phone box (phone boxes are what you see in front of      บ
 บ  your house, and on the side of the street, etc.).  To find a house to     บ
 บ  phreak, you will need to take a look around your neighborhood.  It is     บ
 บ  safest to do it on some old ladies' house who lives close to you.  And    บ
 บ  only do this at night, after 11 pm is always good.  The house should be   บ
 บ  somewhat close to your house, because you don't want to have to walk      บ
 บ  through a big neighborhood late at night, especially if you are under     บ
 บ  18, because the cops will stop you and ask you what you are doing, and    บ
 บ  ask you what's in your back pack.  It would really suck to have to open   บ
 บ  your bag and pull out a beige-box for the cop.  And they get pissed and   บ
 บ  tell you to go home.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once you have found a house, be aware of your surroundings.  Be sure  บ
 บ  there are not people, feds, and pac-bell workers around.  Now you will    บ
 บ  need to go to the side of the house, where the utilities are.  The        บ
 บ  utilities consist of the fuse box, television, and TELEPHONE!.  You       บ
 บ  should see two panels, one labeled "television", and one labeled          บ
 บ  "telephone" with a little bell logo on it.  As I hope you already have    บ
 บ  figured out, we will be using the one that says "telephone."  Using a     บ
 บ  flathead screwdriver, take off the panel, and you should see a grey       บ
 บ  rubber covering.  Take the rubber covering off, and you will see a small  บ
 บ  black box with 4 screws sticking out or you might see 4 bolts sticking    บ
 บ  out.  Now take your alligator clips and clip them both onto 2 of the 4    บ
 บ  screws.  Now plug the phone cord into the phone, pick up the phone, and   บ
 บ  you should now have a dial tone!                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you do not have a dial tone, you may not have connected the phone  บ
 บ  cord wires to the alligator clips correctly, or you may need to           บ
 บ  re-adjust the alligator clips onto the screw, or try the other 2 screws.  บ
 บ  You can now call wherever you want and it doesn't cost you a penny.  To   บ
 บ  find out the number that you are calling from, call 1-800-MY-ANI-IS.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When you are done, make SURE that you cover up your tracks, so        บ
 บ  suspision of your presence does not arouse.  I ususally crank-call        บ
 บ  people in New York (I am in California by the way) and fuck with them.    บ
 บ  Another cool thing to do is call up some 900 numbers.  Boy those numbers  บ
 บ  really get expensive.  I've seen $7.50 per MINUTE.  But who gives a       บ
 บ  fuck, you don't have to pay for it.  Harrassing the operator is also      บ
 บ  fun.  Have fun my fellow phreaks.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Subject : Blowing Up the World 9 Times?                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ      Why did I write this?  I thought RCN may need a relief breaker from   บ
 บ  all of the usual stuff.  Do not take the following list too seriously.    บ
 บ  Heheheh... I just thought of this stuff up.  And by the way.  The Quiet   บ
 บ  Riot, go take that lame group NFS (Need for Speed) and shove it up your   บ
 บ  ass.  That so called ripped install.exe was used by a group!  So go       บ
 บ  fucking steal a life.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As we know, the world has enough nuclear missles to blow up the       บ
 บ  world exactly 9 times.  The following are the top ten reasons why we      บ
 บ  can't blow up the world 9 times :                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  THE TOP TEN LIST!                                                         บ
 บ  -----------------                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      10.) If the world blew up, where would we get hot dogs?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      9.)  Because I want to live!                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      8.)  Rebel Chicken is still a virgin!                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      7.)  We can't find the key to unlock the failsafes on the missles.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      6.)  We got alien invaders in my backyard stealing all the            บ
 บ           plutonium!                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.)  We have to wait until July 4th.  I want to see the movie         บ
 บ           Independance Day.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.)  Your mother is so fat that she would shield part of the world    บ
 บ           from the explosion.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.)  Once you blow up the world once, you can't blow it up again!     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.)  Damned President Clinton already sold all of our nuclear         บ
 บ           weapons to the Communist Soviets.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  And the number 1 reason is :                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.)  There wouldn't be any more RCNs made! ;)                         บ

 บ      RCN is proud to present to the scene the official RCN t-shirt.  We    บ
 บ  tried to keep the price as low as we could so that everyone can enjoy     บ
 บ  these goodies.  Keeping with RCN's volunteerish spirit to help the scene, บ
 บ  Road Rebel has decided to take it upon himself to make the RCN t-shirts   บ
 บ  available to the masses.  This is a non-profit venture and we hope that   บ
 บ  in many ways, RCN continues to benefit the scene.. even when we are not   บ
 บ  near our computers.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       The RCN logo is approximately 8"x6" printed on the back of a        บ
 บ        HEAVY-duty Fruit of the Loom white t-shirt, the front is plain.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       A preview of the shirt can viewed upon pressing escape.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Special orders take up to 4 weeks for shipping.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Summary :                                                                 บ
 บ  ---------                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1.) All RCN issues must be online and available for FREE download.  The   บ
 บ      current issue and back issues must be located in separate file        บ
 บ      directories.  The FULL file_id.diz for the current issue must be      บ
 บ      shown.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2.) A "Reality Check Network" conference must be set up.  The "rcn        บ
 บ      affiliate board" ansi must be shown somewhere in the login process    บ
 บ      or somewhere in the conference join.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3.) Sysops must notify all bulletin board users, via nonconference        บ
 บ      specific mass email, of the new issues available for free download.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The new update to the Reality Check Network World Wide Web Site,      บ
 บ  http://www.rcn.org/, adds many new features :                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Speed Optimization : RCN.org is now speed optimized, which means    บ
 บ        you spend less time waiting and more time browsing.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Back Issue Access : It's now quick and easy to scan through  บ
 บ        RCN's back issues, each one has its full description online, to     บ
 บ        make searching for the desired issue that much easier.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Interface : v2.0 brings an end to the confusing              บ
 บ        conglomeration of pages that previously had existed.  Now speed     บ
 บ        through the icon driven interface to scan back issues of RCN and    บ
 บ        other emags, send comments, read credits, and check out             บ
 บ        merchandise and free files.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Text or JAVA Version : Whatever browser you use can now access the  บ
 บ        RCN.org pages.  Before only Netscape was allowed, but now LYNX and  บ
 บ        other text base users can now access the pages.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       New Look Graphics : The new graphics style are a nice change of     บ
 บ        pace from the hard-edged style of before.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To become a file mirror, contact us in #RCN on IRC, you must be able  บ
 บ  to store all back issues in a publically accessible directory from the    บ
 บ  WWW.  A link will be created from RCN.org to your site, so users can      บ
 บ  acquire issues from there if the main site becomes overloaded.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN WWW Site       : http://www.rcn.org/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN Mirror Site #1 : http://www.halcyon.com/sbecker                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
